<token id="chien">1<token_alt_name>Ch'ien</token_alt_name> / <token_name>The Creative</token_name>

above CH'IEN THE CREATIVE, HEAVEN
below CH'IEN THE CREATIVE, HEAVEN

<protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, line.n.04, unbroken.a.01">The first hexagram is made up of six unbroken lines.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="line.n.04, power.n.01, light.n.02, activity.n.01, strength.n.01, spirit.n.01">These unbroken lines stand for the primal power, which is light-giving, active, strong, and of the spirit.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, strength.n.01, character.n.03, weakness.n.01">The hexagram is consistently strong in character, and since it is without weakness,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="kernel.n.02, power.n.01, energy.n.01">its essence is power or energy.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, image.n.01">Its image is heaven.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="energy.n.01, motion.n.03">Its energy is represented as unrestricted by any fixed conditions in space and is therefore conceived of as motion.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="time.n.01, motion.n.03">Time is regarded as the basis of this motion.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, power.n.01, time.n.01, duration.n.01">Thus the hexagram includes also the power of time and the power of persisting in time, that is, duration.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="power.n.01, hexagram.n.01, sense.n.03, action.n.01, universe.n.01, world.n.01, man.n.01">The power represented by the hexagram is to be interpreted in a dual sense in terms of its action on the universe and of its action on the world of men.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="universe.n.01, hexagram.n.01, action.n.01, deity.n.01">In relation to the universe, the hexagram expresses the strong, creative action of the Deity.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="world.n.01, man.n.01, hexagram.n.01, action.n.01, sage.n.01, ruler.n.01, leader.n.01, power.n.01, nature.n.01">In relation to the human world, it denotes the creative action of the holy man or sage, of the ruler or leader of men, who through his power awakens and develops their higher nature.</apodosis>


THE JUDGMENT

<protasis wn_only="creativity.n.01, work.n.01, sublimity.n.01, success.n.01">THE CREATIVE works sublime success</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="advancement.n.01, perseverance.n.01">Furthering through perseverance</apodosis>.

According to the original meaning, the attributes <protasis wn_only="sublimity.n.01, potentiality.n.01, success.n.03, power.n.01, advancement.n.01, perseverance.n.01">[sublimity, potentiality of success, power to further, perseverance]</protasis> are paired. <apodosis wn_only="person.n.01, drawing.n.01, oracle.n.02, meaning.n.01, success.n.03, universe.n.01, happiness.n.01, perseverance.n.01, morality.n.01">When an individual draws this oracle, it means that success will come to him from the primal depths of the universe and that everything depends upon his seeking his happiness and that of others in one way only, that is, by perseverance in what is right.</apodosis> The specific meanings of the four attributes became the subject of speculation at an early date. The Chinese word here rendered by "sublime" means literally "head," "origin," "great." This is why Confucius says in explaining it: <protasis wn_only="greatness.n.01, generative_power.n.01, creativity.n.01, being.n.01, beginning.n.01">Great indeed is the generating power of the Creative; all beings owe their beginning to it.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="power.n.01, permeation.n.01, heaven.n.01">This power permeates all heaven.</apodosis> For this attribute inheres in the other three as well. <protasis wn_only="beginning.n.01, thing.n.12, form.n.01, idea.n.01, reality.n.01">The beginning of all things lies still in the beyond in the form of ideas that have yet to become real.</protasis> But <apodosis wn_only="creativity.n.01, power.n.01, form.n.01, archetype.n.01, idea.n.01">the Creative furthermore has power to lend form to these archetypes of ideas.</apodosis> This is indicated in the word success, and the process is represented by an image from nature: <protasis wn_only="cloud.n.02, passage.n.03, rain.n.01, work.n.01, being.n.01, flow.n.01, form.n.01">"The clouds pass and the rain does its work, and all individual beings flow into their forms."</protasis> Applies to the human world, these attributes show the great man the way to notable success: <protasis wn_only="sight.n.05, clarity.n.01, cause.n.01, effect.n.01, completion.n.01, step.n.01, time.n.05, mounting.n.02, heaven.n.01, time.n.05, dragon.n.01">“Because he sees with great clarity and cause and effects, he completes the six steps at the right time and mounts toward heaven on them at the right time, as though on six dragons.”</protasis> The six steps are the six different positions given in the hexagram, which are represented later by the dragon symbol. Here it is shown that <apodosis wn_only="way.n.02, success.n.03, apprehension.n.02, actuality.n.02, way.n.04, universe.n.01, law.n.01, end.n.04, beginning.n.01, phenomenon.n.01, time.n.01">the way to success lies in apprehending and giving actuality to the way of the universe [Tao], which, as a law running through end and beginning, brings about all phenomena in time.</apodosis> Thus <apodosis wn_only="step.n.01, attainment.n.01, preparation.n.01">each step attained forthwith becomes a preparation for the next.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="time.n.01, hindrance.n.01, means.n.01, actuality.n.01, potentiality.n.01">Time is no longer a hindrance but the means of making actual what is potential.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="act.n.02, creation.n.01, expression.n.02, attribute.n.02, sublimity.n.01, success.n.03">The act of creation having found expression in the two attributes sublimity and success</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="work.n.01, preservation.n.02, actualization.n.02, differentiation.n.03, form.n.01">the work of conservation is shown to be a continuous actualization and differentiation of form.</apodosis> This is expressed in the two terms <protasis wn_only="advancement.n.01, creation.n.01, accordance.n.01, nature.n.01, being.n.01">“furthering” (literally, “creating that which accords with the nature of a given being”)</protasis> and <protasis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, correctness.n.01, firmness.n.01">“persevering” (literally, “correct and firm”).</protasis> <protasis wn_only="course.n.01, creativity.n.01, alteration.n.01, shape.n.02, being.n.01, attainment.n.01, truth.n.01, specificity.n.01, nature.n.01">“The course of the Creative alters and shapes beings until each attains its true, specific nature</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="conformity.n.01, great_harmony.n.01">then it keeps them in conformity with the Great Harmony.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="demonstration.n.02, advancement.n.01, perseverance.n.01">Thus does it show itself to further through perseverance.”</apodosis> In relation to the human sphere, this shows how <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, peace.n.01, security.n.01, world.n.01, activity.n.01, creation.n.01, order.n.01">the great man brings peace and security to the world through his activity in creating order</apodosis>: <protasis wn_only="tower.v.01, multitude.n.01, being.n.01, land.n.04, union.n.01, peace.n.01">"He towers high above the multitude of beings, and all lands are united in peace."</protasis> Another line of speculation goes still further in separating the words “sublime,” “success,” “furthering,” “perseverance,” and parallels them with the four cardinal virtues in humanity. To sublimity, which, as the fundamental principle, embraces all the other attributes, it links love. To the attribute success are linked the morals, which regulate and organize expressions of love and thereby make them successful. The attribute furthering is correlated with justice, which creates the conditions in which each receives that which accords with his being, that which is due him and which constitutes his happiness. The attribute perseverance is correlated with wisdom, which discerns the immutable laws of all that happens and can therefore bring about enduring conditions. These speculations, already broached in the commentary called Wên Yen , later formed the bridge connecting the philosophy of the “five stages (elements) of change,” as laid down in the Book of History (Shu Ching) with the philosophy of the Book of Changes, which is based solely on the polarity of positive and negative principles. In the course of time this combination of the two systems of thought opened the way for an increasingly intricate number symbolism.


THE IMAGE

<protasis wn_only="motion.n.06, heaven.n.01">The movement of heaven</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="power.n.01">is full of power</apodosis>.
Thus <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, strength.n.01">the superior man makes himself strong</apodosis> and
<apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, indefatigability.n.01">untiring</apodosis>.

Since <protasis wn_only="heaven.n.01, unity.n.01">there is only one heaven</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="trigram.n.01, doubling.n.02, heaven.n.01, image.n.01">the doubling of the trigram Ch’ien, of which heaven is the image</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="motion.n.06, heaven.n.01">indicates the movement of heaven</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="revolution.n.02, heaven.n.01, day.n.01">One complete revolution of heaven makes a day</protasis>, and <apodosis wn_only="trigram.n.01, repetition.n.02, day.n.01, sequence.n.01">the repetition of the trigram means that each day is followed by another</apodosis>. This <apodosis wn_only="time.n.05, idea.n.01">creates the idea of time</apodosis>. Since <protasis wn_only="heaven.n.01, motion.n.06, power.n.01, indefatigability.n.01">it is the same heaven moving with untiring power</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="time.n.05, duration.n.03, idea.n.01">there is also created the idea of duration both in and beyond time</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="motion.n.06, cessation.n.01">a movement that never stops nor slackens</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="day.n.01, sequence.n.01">just as one day follows another in an unending course</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="time.n.05, duration.n.03, image.n.01, power.n.01">This duration in time is the image of the power inherent in the Creative</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="image.n.01, model.n.02">With this image as a model</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="sage.n.01, development.n.01">the sage learns how best to develop himself</apodosis> so that <apodosis wn_only="influence.n.01, duration.n.03">his influence may endure</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="strength.n.01">He must make himself strong in every way</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="rejection.n.01, inferiority.n.01, degradation.n.01">by consciously casting out all that is inferior and degrading</apodosis>. Thus <apodosis wn_only="indefatigability.n.01, limitation.n.01, field.n.01, activity.n.01">he attains that tirelessness which depends upon consciously limiting the fields of his activity</apodosis>.


THE LINES


Nine at the beginning means:
<protasis wn_only="dragon.n.01">Hidden dragon</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="action.n.01, inaction.n.01">Do not act</apodosis>.

In China the <protasis wn_only="dragon.n.01, symbol.n.01">dragon has a meaning altogether different from that given it in the Western world</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="dragon.n.01, symbol.n.01, electricity.n.01, force.n.01, thunderstorm.n.01">The dragon is a symbol of the electrically charged, dynamic, arousing force that manifests itself in the thunderstorm</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="winter.n.01, energy.n.01, withdrawal.n.01, earth.n.01">In winter this energy withdraws into the earth</protasis>; <apodosis wn_only="summer.n.01, activation.n.01, sky.n.01, thunder.n.02, lightning.n.01">in the early summer it becomes active again, appearing in the sky as thunder and lightning</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="creation.n.02, force.n.01, earth.n.01, beginning.n.01">As a result the creative forces on earth begin to stir again</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="force.n.01, concealment.n.01, earth.n.01">Here this creative force is still hidden beneath the earth</protasis> and therefore <apodosis wn_only="effect.n.01, absence.n.01">has no effect</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="person.n.01, greatness.n.01, recognition.n.01, lack.n.01">In terms of human affairs, this symbolizes a great man who is still unrecognized</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="truth.n.01, self.n.01">Nonetheless he remains true to himself</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="influence.n.01, success.n.03, failure.n.01, permission.n.01, refusal.n.01">He does not allow himself to be influenced by outward success or failure</apodosis>, but <protasis wn_only="confidence.n.01, strength.n.01">confident in his strength</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="time.n.05, waiting.n.01">he bides his time</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="wisdom.n.01, person.n.01, oracle.n.02, drawing.n.01, waiting.n.01, strength.n.01, patience.n.01">Hence it is wise for the man who consults the oracle and draws this line to wait in the calm strength of patience</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="time.n.05, fulfillment.n.01">The time will fulfill itself</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="fear.n.01, necessity.n.01, strength.n.01, prevalence.n.01">One need not fear least strong will should not prevail</apodosis>; <apodosis wn_only="importance.n.01, expenditure.n.01, power.n.01, prematurity.n.01, attempt.n.01, force.n.01, acquisition.n.01, time.n.05, ripeness.n.01">the main thing is not to expend one’s powers prematurely in an attempt to obtain by force something for which the time is not yet ripe</apodosis>.


Nine in the second place means:
<protasis wn_only="dragon.n.01, field.n.01, appearance.n.01">Dragon appearing in the field.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="benefit.n.01, man.n.01, appearance.n.01">It furthers one to see the great man.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="light.n.06, power.n.01, manifestation.n.02">Here the effects of the light-giving power begin to manifest themselves.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="human.n.01, affair.n.01, man.n.01, appearance.n.01, field.n.01, activity.n.01">In terms of human affairs, this means that the great man makes his appearance in his chosen field of activity.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="position.n.01, peer.n.01">As yet he has no commanding position but is still with his peers.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, seriousness.n.01, purpose.n.01, reliability.n.01, influence.n.01, environment.n.01, effort.n.01">However, what distinguishes him form the others is his seriousness of purpose, his unqualified reliability, and the influence he exerts on his environment with out conscious effort.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, destiny.n.01, influence.n.01, world.n.01, order.n.01">Such a man is destined to gain great influence and to set the world in order.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="benefit.n.01, man.n.01, appearance.n.01">Therefore it is favorable to see him.</apodosis>


Nine in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, superior.n.01, day.n.01">All day long the superior man is creatively active.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="night.n.01, mind.n.01, concern.n.01">At nightfall his mind is still beset with cares.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="danger.n.01, blame.n.01">Danger. No blame.</apodosis>

<apodosis wn_only="sphere.n.01, influence.n.01, man.n.01">A sphere of influence opens up for the great man.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="fame.n.01">His fame begins to spread.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="mass.n.01">The masses flock to him.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="power.n.01, activity.n.01">His inner power is adequate to the increased outer activity.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="thing.n.12, evening.n.01">There are all sorts of things to be done, and when others are at rest in the evening,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="plan.n.01, anxiety.n.01">plans and anxieties press in upon him.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="danger.n.01, place.n.01, transition.n.01, lowliness.n.01, height.n.01">But danger lurks here at the place of transition from lowliness to the heights.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, mass.n.01, course.n.01, ambition.n.01, integrity.n.01">Many a great man has been ruined because the masses flocked to him and swept him into their course. Ambition has destroyed his integrity.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="greatness.n.01, temptation.n.01">However, true greatness is not impaired by temptations.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="time.n.05, demand.n.01">He who remains in touch with the time that is dawning, and with its demands</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="prudence.n.01, pitfall.n.01, blamelessness.n.01">is prudent enough to avoid all pitfalls, and remains blameless.</apodosis>


Nine in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="flight.n.01, depth.n.01, wavering.n.01">Wavering flight over the depths.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="blameworthiness.n.01">No blame.</apodosis>

<apodosis wn_only="topographic_point.n.01, transition.n.01">A place of transition has been reached</apodosis>, and <apodosis wn_only="choice.n.01">free choice can enter in</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="possibility.n.01">A twofold possibility is presented to the great man</apodosis>: <apodosis wn_only="soaring.n.01, height.n.01, role.n.01, world.n.01">he can soar to the heights and play an important part in the world</apodosis>, or <apodosis wn_only="withdrawal.n.01, solitude.n.01, development.n.01">he can withdraw into solitude and develop himself</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="way.n.01, hero.n.01">He can go the way of the hero</apodosis> or <apodosis wn_only="way.n.01, sage.n.01, seclusion.n.01">that of the holy sage who seeks seclusion</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="law.n.01">There is no general law of his being.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="individual.n.01, action.n.01, consistency.n.01, truth.n.01">If the individual acts consistently and is true to himself</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="way.n.01">he will find the way that is appropriate for him</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="way.n.01, rightness.n.01, blameworthiness.n.01">This way is right for him and without blame.</apodosis>

Nine in the fifth place means:
<protasis wn_only="dragon.n.01, sky.n.01">Flying dragon in the heavens.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="benefit.n.01, man.n.01">It furthers one to see the great man.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, sphere.n.04, being.n.02">Here the great man has attained the sphere of the heavenly beings.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="influence.n.01, world.n.01, visibility.n.01">His influence spreads and becomes visible throughout the whole world.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="blessing.n.01">Everyone who sees him may count himself blessed.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="tone.n.01, accord.n.01">Things that accord in tone vibrate together.</protasis>
<protasis wn_only="affinity.n.01, nature.n.01">Things that have affinity in their inmost natures seek one another.</protasis>
<protasis wn_only="water.n.01, wetness.n.01">Water flows to what is wet,</protasis>
<protasis wn_only="fire.n.01, dryness.n.01">fire turns to what is dry.</protasis>
<protasis wn_only="cloud.n.02, breath.n.01, dragon.n.01">Clouds (the breath of heaven) follow the dragon,</protasis>
<protasis wn_only="wind.n.01, breath.n.01, tiger.n.01">wind (the breath of earth) follows the tiger.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="sage.n.01, creature.n.01">Thus the sage arises, and all creatures follow him with their eyes.</apodosis>
<protasis wn_only="birth.n.02, heaven.n.01">What is born of heaven feels related to what is above.</protasis>
<protasis wn_only="birth.n.02, earth.n.01">What is born of earth feels related to what is below.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="kind.n.01">Each follows its kind.</apodosis>

Nine at the top means:

<apodosis wn_only="dragon.n.01, arrogance.n.01, repentance.n.01">Arrogant dragon will have cause to repent.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, isolation.n.01, mankind.n.01">When a man seeks to climb so high that he loses touch with the rest of mankind, he becomes isolated,</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="failure.n.01">and this necessarily leads to failure.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="warning.n.01, aspiration.n.01, power.n.01">This line warns against titanic aspirations that exceed one's power.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="fall.n.06">A precipitous fall would follow.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="line.n.05">When all the lines are nines,</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="dragon.n.01, flight.n.01, head.n.01">There appears a flight of dragons without heads.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.01">Good fortune.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="line.n.05">When all the lines are nines,</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, motion.n.06, change.n.02, devotion.n.02">it means that the whole hexagram is in motion and changes into the hexagram K'un, THE RECEPTIVE, whose character is devotion.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="strength.n.01, mildness.n.01, unity.n.01">The strength of the Creative and the mildness of the Receptive unite.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="strength.n.01, dragon.n.01, flight.n.01">Strength is indicated by the flight of dragons,</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="mildness.n.01, head.n.01, concealment.n.02">mildness by the fact that their heads are hidden.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="mildness.n.01, action.n.01, strength.n.01, decision.n.01, fortune.n.01">This means that mildness in action joined to strength of decision brings good fortune.</apodosis>

<token id="kun">2<token_alt_name>K'un</token_alt_name> / <token_name>The Receptive</token_name>

above K’UN THE RECEPTIVE, EARTH
below K’UN THE RECEPTIVE, EARTH

<protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, line.n.04">This hexagram is made up of broken lines only</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="line.n.04, yin.n.01, power.n.01">The broken lines represents the dark, yielding, receptive primal power of yin</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, attribute.n.02, devotion.n.01">The attribute of the hexagram is devotion</apodosis>; <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, image.n.01, earth.n.01">its image is the earth</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, complement.n.01">It is the perfect complement of THE CREATIVE--the complement, not the opposite</apodosis>, <protasis wn_only="receptive.n.01, creative.n.01, combat.n.01, completion.n.01">for the Receptive does not combat the Creative but completes it</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, nature.n.01, spirit.n.01, earth.n.01, heaven.n.01, space.n.01, time.n.05, female.n.01, male.n.01">It represents nature in contrast to spirit, earth in contrast to heaven, space as against time, the female-maternal as against the male-paternal</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="principle.n.01, human.n.01, affair.n.01, relation.n.01, man.n.01, woman.n.01, prince.n.01, minister.n.03, father.n.01, son.n.01">However, as applied to human affairs, the principle of this complementary relationship is found not only in the relation between man and woman, but also in that between prince and minister and between father and son</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="duality.n.01, individual.n.01, world.n.08, world.n.09">Indeed, even in the individual this duality appears in the coexistence of the spiritual world and the world of the senses</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="dualism.n.02, hierarchical.s.01, relationship.n.01, principle.n.01">But strictly speaking there is no real dualism here, because there is a clearly defined hierarchic relationship between the two principles</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="receptive.n.01, creative.n.01, attribute.n.02, devotion.n.01, place.n.01, power.n.01, relation.n.01">In itself of course the Receptive is just as important as the Creative, but the attribute of devotion defines the place occupied by this primal power in relation to the Creative</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="receptive.n.01, activation.n.02, creative.n.01, production.n.01">For the Receptive must be activated and led by the Creative; then it is productive of good</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="receptive.n.01, position.n.01, equality.n.01, creative.n.01">Only when it abandons this position and tries to stand as an equal side by side with the Creative</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="evil.n.01">does it become evil</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="opposition.n.01, struggle.n.01, creative.n.01, production.n.01, evil.n.01">The result then is opposition to and struggle against the Creative, which is productive of evil to both</apodosis>.

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="receptive.n.01, success.n.01">THE RECEPTIVE brings about sublime success,</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="advancement.n.01, perseverance.n.01, mare.n.01">Furthering through the perseverance of a mare.</apodosis>
<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, superior.n.01, undertaking.n.01, leadership.n.01">If the superior man undertakes something and tries to lead,</protasis>

THE IMAGE

<protasis wn_only="earth.n.01, condition.n.01, receptivity.n.01, devotion.n.01">The earth’s condition is receptive devotion.</protasis>

<protasis wn_only="heaven.n.01, earth.n.01, hexagram.n.01, trigram.n.01, duration.n.01, time.n.05, solidity.n.01, extension.n.02, space.n.01">Just as there is only one heaven, so too there is only one earth. In the hexagram of heaven the doubling of the trigram implies duration in time, but in the hexagram of earth the doubling connotes the solidity and extension in space by virtue of which the earth is able to carry and preserve all things that live and move upon it.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="earth.n.01, devotion.n.01, man.n.01, character.n.01, breadth.n.01, purity.n.01, power.n.01, people.n.01, thing.n.01">The earth in its devotion carries all things, good and evil,, without exception. In the same way the superior man gives to his character breadth, purity, and sustaining power, so that he is able both to support and to bear with people and things.</apodosis>

Six in the fifth place means:

<protasis wn_only="garment.n.01, yellow.n.01">A yellow lower garment</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.01, supremacy.n.01, goodness.n.01">supreme good fortune</apodosis>.

Yellow is the color of the earth and of the middle; it is the symbol of that which is <apodosis wn_only="reliability.n.01, genuineness.n.01">reliable and genuine</apodosis>. The lower garment is inconspicuously decorated--the symbol of <apodosis wn_only="aristocracy.n.01, reserve.n.04">aristocratic reserve</apodosis>. When anyone is called upon to work in a prominent but not independent position, <apodosis wn_only="success.n.01, discretion.n.01">true success depends on the utmost discretion</apodosis>. A man’s <apodosis wn_only="genuineness.n.01, refinement.n.01">genuineness and refinement</apodosis> should not reveal themselves directly; they should express themselves only indirectly as an effect from within.

Six at the top means:

<protasis wn_only="dragon.n.01, fight.n.01, meadow.n.01">Dragons fight in the meadow</protasis>.
<apodosis wn_only="blood.n.01, black.n.01, yellow.n.01">Their blood is black and yellow</apodosis>.

In the top place the dark element should yield to the light. If it attempts to maintain a position to which it is not entitled and to rule instead of serving, it draws down upon itself the anger of the strong. A struggle ensues in which it is overthrown, with injury, however, to both sides. The dragon, symbol of heaven, comes to fight the false dragon that symbolized the inflation of the earth principle. <apodosis wn_only="midnight.n.01, blue.n.01, color.n.01, heaven.n.01">Midnight blue is the color of heaven</apodosis>; <apodosis wn_only="yellow.n.01, color.n.01, earth.n.01">yellow is the color of earth</apodosis>. Therefore, when <protasis wn_only="black.n.01, yellow.n.01, blood.n.01, flow.n.01">black and yellow blood flow</protasis>, it is <apodosis wn_only="sign.n.02, contest.n.01, unnaturalness.n.01, injury.n.01">a sign that in this unnatural contest both primal powers suffer injury</apodosis>.

When all the lines are sixes, it means:

<apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, duration.n.01">Lasting perseverance furthers</apodosis>.

When <protasis wn_only="six.n.01">nothing but sixes appears</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, change.n.01">the hexagram of THE RECEPTIVE changes into the hexagram of THE CREATIVE</apodosis>. By <protasis wn_only="holding.n.01, rightness.n.01">holding fast to what is right</protasis>, it gains <apodosis wn_only="power.n.01, endurance.n.01">the power of enduring</apodosis>. There is indeed no advance, but neither is there retrogression.

Hence <apodosis wn_only="holding.n.01, back.n.01">he must hold back</apodosis>, because <protasis wn_only="prematurity.n.01, move.n.01">any premature move</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="bringing.n.01, disaster.n.01">might bring disaster</apodosis>. Likewise, <apodosis wn_only="importance.n.01, aloneness.n.01">it is very important not to remain alone</apodosis>; <protasis wn_only="overcoming.n.01, chaos.n.01">in order to overcome the chaos</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="need.n.01, assistant.n.01">he needs helpers</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="image.n.01, difficulty.n.01, beginning.n.01">The image of DIFFICULTY AT THE BEGINNING</apodosis>.

Thus the superior man
<apodosis wn_only="order.n.01, confusion.n.01">Brings order out of confusion</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="cloud.n.01, thunder.n.02">Clouds and thunder</protasis> are represented by definite decorative lines; this means that <apodosis wn_only="chaos.n.01, difficulty.n.01, beginning.n.01, order.n.01">in the chaos of difficulty at the beginning, order is already implicit</apodosis>. THE LINES

Nine at the beginning means:
<protasis wn_only="hesitation.n.01, hindrance.n.01">Hesitation and hindrance.</protasis>

<token id="shih">7<token_alt_name>Shih</token_alt_name> / <token_name>The Army</token_name>

above K’UN THE RECEPTIVE, EARTH
below K’AN THE ABYSMAL, WATER

<protasis wn_only="trigram.n.01, water.n.06, earth.n.01">This hexagram is made up of the trigrams K’an, water, and K’un, earth</protasis>, and thus <apodosis wn_only="groundwater.n.01, earth.n.01">it symbolizes the ground water stored up in the earth</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="military_strength.n.01, people.n.01">In the same way military strength is stored up in the mass of the people</protasis>--<apodosis wn_only="peace.n.01, power.n.01">invisible in times of peace but always ready for use as a source of power</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="trigram.n.01, danger.n.01, obedience.n.01">The attributes of the two trigrams are danger inside and obedience must prevail outside.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="line.n.01, hexagram.n.01, strength.n.01, place.n.01">Of the individual lines, the one that controls the hexagram is the strong nine in the second place</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="subordination.n.01">to which the other lines, all yielding, are subordinate</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="line.n.01, commander.n.01, trigram.n.01">This line indicates a commander, because it stands in the middle of one of the two trigrams.</protasis> But <protasis wn_only="trigram.n.01">since it is in the lower rather than the upper trigram</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="ruler.n.01, general.n.01, obedience.n.01, army.n.01, authority.n.01">it represents not the ruler but the efficient general, who maintains obedience in the army by his authority</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="conduct.n.01">Resolute conduct.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, awareness.n.01, danger.n.01">Perseverance with awareness of danger.</apodosis>

This refers to the ruler of the hexagram as a whole. One sees that one has to be resolute in conduct. But at the same time one must remain conscious of the danger connected with such resoluteness, especially if it is to be persevered in. Only awareness of the danger makes success possible.

Nine at the top means:

<protasis wn_only="conduct.n.01, sign.n.03">Look to your conduct and weigh the favorable signs.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="fulfillment.n.01, fortune.n.01">When everything is fulfilled, supreme good fortune comes.</apodosis>

The work is ended. If we want to know whether good fortune will follow, we must look back upon our conduct and its consequences. If the effects are good, then good fortune is certain. No one knows himself. It is only by the consequences of his actions, by the fruit of his labors, that a man can judge what he is to expect.

<apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03, people.n.01">This means good fortune for inferior people.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="people.n.01, flattery.n.01, manner.n.01">Inferior people are ready to flatter their superiors in a servile way.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, confusion.n.01">They would also endure the superior man if he would put an end to their confusion.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">This is fortunate for them.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, consequence.n.01, standstill.n.01">But the great man calmly bears the consequences of the standstill.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="crowd.n.01">He does not mingle with the crowd of the inferior;</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="place.n.02">that is not his place.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="willingness.n.01, suffering.n.01">By his willingness to suffer personally</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="principle.n.01, success.n.01">he insures the success of his fundamental principles.</apodosis>

Six in the third place means:

<protasis wn_only="shame.n.01">They bear shame.</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="people.n.01, power.n.01, illegitimacy.n.01, responsibility.n.01, inequality.n.01">Inferior people who have risen to power illegitimately do not feel equal to the responsibility they have taken upon themselves.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="heart.n.01, shame.n.01">In their hearts they begin to be ashamed</protasis>, <protasis wn_only="beginning.n.01, outwardness.n.01">although at first they do not show it outwardly.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="turn.n.01, betterment.n.01">This marks a turn for the better.</apodosis>

Nine in the fourth place means:

<protasis wn_only="act.n.01, command.n.01, high.n.01">He who acts at the command of the highest</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="blamelessness.n.01">Remains without blame.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="mind.n.01, similarity.n.01, blessing.n.01, partaking.n.01">Those of like mind partake of the blessing.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="time_period.n.01, standstill.n.01, change.n.01, approach.n.01, opposite.n.01">The time of standstill is nearing the point of change into its opposite.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="desire.n.01, order.n.01, restoration.n.01, feeling.n.01, calling.n.01, task.n.01, authority.n.01, necessity.n.01">Whoever wishes to restore order must feel himself called to the task and have the necessary authority.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, capability.n.01, order.n.01, creation.n.01, judgment.n.01">A man who sets himself up a capable of creating order according to his own judgment</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="error.n.01, failure.n.01">could make mistakes and end in failure.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, calling.n.01, task.n.01">But the man who is truly called to the task</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="favor.n.01, time.n.05, condition.n.01, mind.n.01, similarity.n.01, blessing.n.01, sharing.n.01">is favored by the conditions of the time, and all those of like mind will share in his blessing.</apodosis>

Nine in the fifth place means:

<protasis wn_only="standstill.n.01">Standstill is giving way.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.01, man.n.01">Good fortune for the great man.</apodosis>
<protasis wn_only="failure.n.01">"What if it should fail, what if it should fail?"</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="knot.n.01, cluster.n.01, shoot.n.01, mulberry.n.01">In this way he ties it to a cluster of mulberry shoots.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="time.n.05, change.n.01">The time undergoes a change.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, order.n.01, arrival.n.01">The right man, able to restore order, has arrived.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.01">Hence "good fortune."</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="period.n.01, transition.n.01">But such periods of transition are the very times in which we must fear and tremble.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="success.n.01, caution.n.01">Success is assured only through greatest caution,</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="failure.n.01">which asks always, "What if it should fail?"</protasis> <protasis wn_only="mulberry.n.01, bush.n.01, shoot.n.01, root.n.01">When a mulberry bush is cut down, a number of unusually strong shoots sprout from the roots.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="knot.n.01, cluster.n.01, mulberry.n.01, shoot.n.01, success.n.01, certainty.n.01">Hence the image of tying something to a cluster of mulberry shoots is used to symbolize the way of making success certain.</apodosis>

Confucius says about this line:
<protasis wn_only="danger.n.01, security.n.01">Danger arises when a man feels secure in his position.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="destruction.n.01, estate.n.01">Destruction threatens when a man seeks to preserve his worldly estate.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="confusion.n.01, order.n.01">Confusion develops when a man has put everything in order.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, danger.n.01, security.n.01, ruin.n.01, establishment.n.01, confusion.n.01, order.n.01, safety.n.01, empire.n.01">Therefore the superior man does not forget danger in his security, not ruin when he is well established, nor confusion when his affairs are in order. In this way he gains personal safety and is able to protect the empire.</apodosis>

Nine at the top means:

<protasis wn_only="standstill.n.01, end.n.04">The standstill comes to an end.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="standstill.n.01, fortune.n.01">First standstill, then good fortune.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="standstill.n.01, perpetuity.n.01">The standstill does not last forever.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="cessation.n.01, man.n.01">However, it does not cease of its own accord; the right man is needed to end it.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="peace.n.01, stagnation.n.01">This is the difference between a state of peace and a state of stagnation.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="effort.n.01, peace.n.01">Continuous effort is necessary to maintain peace:</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="stagnation.n.01, disintegration.n.01">left to itself it would change into stagnation and disintegration.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="disintegration.n.01, peace.n.01, prosperity.n.01">The time of disintegration, however, does not change back automatically to a condition of peace and prosperity;</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="effort.n.01, end.n.04">effort must be put forth in order to end it.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="attitude.n.01, world.n.01, order.n.01">This shows the creative attitude that man must take if the world is to be put in order.</apodosis>

7. <protasis wn_only="danger.n.01, obedience.n.01, character.n.01, army.n.01">In the latter, danger is within and obedience without--the character of a warlike army,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="cohesion.n.01, man.n.01, weakness.n.01">which, in order to hold together, needs one strong man among the many who are weak.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="clarity.n.01, strength.n.01, character.n.01, union.n.01, man.n.01">Here, clarity is within and strength without--the character of a peaceful union of men,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="cohesion.n.01, nature.n.01, person.n.01, firmness.n.01">which, in order to hold together, needs one yielding nature among many firm persons.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="fellowship.n.01, man.n.01, open.n.01">FELLOWSHIP WITH MEN in the open.</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, man.n.01">The perseverance of the superior man furthers.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="fellowship.n.01, man.n.01, concern.n.01, universality.n.01">True fellowship among men must be based upon a concern that is universal.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="interest.n.01, individual.n.01, fellowship.n.01, man.n.01, lastingness.n.01">It is not the private interests of the individual that create lasting fellowship among men,</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="goal.n.01, humanity.n.01">but rather the goals of humanity.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="fellowship.n.01, man.n.01, open.n.01, success.n.03">That is why it is said that fellowship with men in the open succeeds.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="unity.n.01, prevalence.n.01">If unity of this kind prevails,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="task.n.01, difficulty.n.01, danger.n.01, water.n.06, accomplishment.n.01">even difficult and dangerous tasks, such as crossing the great water, can be accomplished.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="fellowship.n.01, leader.n.01, perseverance.n.01, enlightenment.n.02, need.n.01, man.n.01, clarity.n.01, aim.n.01, convincingness.n.01, inspiration.n.02, strength.n.01">But in order to bring about this sort of fellowship, a persevering and enlightened leader is needed--a man with clear, convincing, and inspiring aims and the strength to carry them out.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="trigram.n.01, clarity.n.01, strength.n.01">(The inner trigram means clarity; the outer, strength.)</apodosis>

THE IMAGE

<apodosis wn_only="beginning.n.01, union.n.01, people.n.01, door.n.01">The beginning of union among people should take place before the door.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="equality.n.01, closeness.n.01">All are equally close to one another.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="aim.n.01">No divergent aims have yet arisen,</apodosis> and <apodosis wn_only="mistake.n.01">one makes not mistakes.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="principle.n.01, union.n.01, accessibility.n.01">The basic principles of any kind of union must be equally accessible to all concerned.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="agreement.n.01, misfortune.n.01">Secret agreements bring misfortune.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="fellowship.n.01, man.n.01, clan.n.01">Fellowship with men in the clan.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="humiliation.n.01">Humiliation.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="danger.n.01, formation.n.01, faction.n.01, basis.n.02, interest.n.01, person.n.01, egotism.n.01">There is danger here of formation of a separate faction on the basis of personal and egotistic interests.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="faction.n.01, exclusiveness.n.01, welcome.n.01, man.n.01, condemnation.n.01, group.n.01, union.n.05, motive.n.01, humiliation.n.01, time.n.05">Such factions, which are exclusive and, instead of welcoming all men, must condemn one group in order to unite the others, originate from low motives and therefore lead in the course of time to humiliation.</apodosis>

Nine in the third place means:

<protasis wn_only="weapon.n.01, thicket.n.01, concealment.n.01">He hides weapons in the thicket</protasis>;

<apodosis wn_only="year.n.01, inaction.n.01">For three years he does not rise up</apodosis>.

<apodosis wn_only="fellowship.n.01, change.n.01, mistrust.n.01">Here fellowship has changed about to mistrust</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, distrust.n.01">Each man distrusts the other</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="plan.n.01, ambush.n.01, secrecy.n.01">plans a secret ambush</apodosis>, and <apodosis wn_only="spying.n.01, distance.n.01">seeks to spy on his fellow form afar</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="opposition.n.01, obstinacy.n.01, method.n.01, inefficacy.n.01">We are dealing with an obstinate opponent whom we cannot come at by this method</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="obstacle.n.01, fellowship.n.01">Obstacles standing in the way of fellowship with others are shown here</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="reservation.n.02">One has mental reservations for one’s own part</protasis> and <apodosis wn_only="surprise.n.01, opponent.n.01">seeks to take his opponent by surprise</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="mistrust.n.01, suspicion.n.01, wile.n.01, opponent.n.01">This very fact makes one mistrustful, suspecting the same wiles in his opponent and trying to ferret them out</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="departure.n.01, fellowship.n.01, alienation.n.01">The result is that one departs further and further from true fellowship</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="duration.n.01, alienation.n.01">The longer this goes on, the more alienated one becomes</apodosis>.

Nine in the fourth place means:

<protasis wn_only="climb.n.01, wall.n.01">He climbs up on his wall</protasis>; <apodosis wn_only="attack.n.01, inability.n.01">he cannot attack</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">Good fortune</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="reconciliation.n.01, quarrel.n.02">Here the reconciliation that follows quarrel</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="change_of_location.n.01">mover nearer</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="truth.n.03, wall.n.01">It is true that there are still dividing walls</protasis> <protasis wn_only="confrontation.n.01">on which we stand confronting one another</protasis>. But <protasis wn_only="difficulty.n.01">the difficulties are too great</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="strait.n.01">We get into straits</apodosis>, and <apodosis wn_only="sense.n.03">this brings us to our senses</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="fight.n.01, inability.n.01">We cannot fight</apodosis>, and <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">therein lies our good fortune</apodosis>.

Nine in the fifth place means:

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, fellowship.n.02, tear.n.01, lamentation.n.02">Men bound in fellowship first weep and lament</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="laughter.n.01">But afterward they laugh</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="struggle.n.02, success.n.01, meeting.n.01">After great struggles they succeed in meeting</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="people.n.01, separation.n.01, heart.n.01, unity.n.01">Two people are outwardly separated, but in their hearts they are united</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="position.n.01, life.n.01, separation.n.01">They are kept apart by their positions in life</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="difficulty.n.01, obstruction.n.01, sorrow.n.01">Many difficulties and obstructions arise between them and cause them grief</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="loyalty.n.01, separation.n.01">But, remaining true to each other, the allow nothing to separate them</protasis>, and <apodosis wn_only="struggle.n.02, obstacle.n.01, success.n.01">although it costs them a severe struggle to overcome the obstacles, they will succeed</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="meeting.n.01, sadness.n.01, joy.n.01">When they come together their sadness will change to joy</apodosis>. Confucius says of this:

<apodosis wn_only="life.n.01, man.n.01, path.n.04, winding.n.01">Life leads the thoughtful man on a path of many windings</apodosis>.<apodosis wn_only="course.n.01, check.n.01">Now the course is checked</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="course.n.01">now it runs straight again</apodosis>.<apodosis wn_only="thought.n.01, word.n.01">Here winged thoughts may pour freely forth in words</apodosis>,<apodosis wn_only="burden.n.01, knowledge.n.01, silence.n.01">There the heavy burden of knowledge must be shut away in silence</apodosis>.<protasis wn_only="people.n.01, unity.n.01, heart.n.01">But when two people are at one in the inmost hearts</protasis>,<apodosis wn_only="strength.n.01, iron.n.01, bronze.n.01">They shatter even the strength of iron or of bronze</apodosis>.<protasis wn_only="people.n.01, sympathy.n.01, heart.n.01">And when two people understand each other in their inmost hearts</protasis>,<apodosis wn_only="word.n.01, fragrance.n.02, orchid.n.01">Their words are sweet and strong, like the fragrance of orchids</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="fellowship.n.02, man.n.01, meadow.n.01">Fellowship with men in the meadow</protasis>.

<protasis wn_only="fire.n.01, heaven.n.01">Fire in heaven above</protasis>:

THE LINES

Nine at the beginning means:

<protasis wn_only="relationship.n.01, harm.n.01">No relationship with what is harmful</protasis>;
<apodosis wn_only="blame.n.01">There is no blame in this</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="consciousness.n.01, difficulty.n.01">If one remains conscious of difficulty</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="blame.n.01">One remains without blame</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="possession.n.01, beginning.n.01, challenge.n.01">Great possession that is still in its beginnings and that has not yet been challenged</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="blame.n.01, opportunity.n.01, mistake.n.01">brings no blame, since there has been no opportunity to make mistakes</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="difficulty.n.01">Yet there are many difficulties to be overcome</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="consciousness.n.01, difficulty.n.01">It is only by remaining conscious of theses difficulties</protasis> that <apodosis wn_only="freedom.n.01, arrogance.n.01, wastefulness.n.01, principle.n.01, blame.n.01">one can keep inwardly free of possible arrogance and wastefulness, and thus in principle overcome all cause for blame</apodosis>.

Nine in the second place means:

<protasis wn_only="wagon.n.01, size.n.01">A big wagon for loading.</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="music.n.01, virtue.n.01, hero.n.01, bridge.n.01, world.n.01">It fell to music to glorify the virtues of heroes and thus to construct a bridge to the world of the unseen</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="temple.n.01, god.n.01, music.n.01, pantomime.n.01, theater.n.01">In the temple men drew near to God with music and pantomimes (out of this later the theater developed)</protasis>.
<apodosis wn_only="feeling.n.01, creator.n.02, world.n.01, feeling.n.01, ancestor.n.01">Religious feeling for the Creator of the world was united with the most sacred of human feelings, that of reverence for the ancestors</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="ancestor.n.01, deity.n.01, guest.n.01, ruler.n.01, heaven.n.01, representative.n.01, humanity.n.01, region.n.01">The ancestors were invited to these divine services as guests of the Ruler of Heaven and as representatives of humanity in the higher regions</protasis>.
<apodosis wn_only="god.n.01, man.n.01, ruler.n.01, deity.n.01, ancestor.n.01, son.n.01, heaven.n.01, world.n.01, contact.n.01">This uniting of the human past with the Divinity in solemn moments of religious inspiration established the bond between God and man. The ruler who revered the Divinity in revering his ancestors became thereby the Son of Heaven, in whom the heavenly and the earthly world met in mystical contact</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="idea.n.01, summation.n.01, culture.n.01">These ideas are the final summation of Chinese culture</protasis>.
<apodosis wn_only="sacrifice.n.01, rite.n.01, world.n.01, hand.n.01">Confucius has said of the great sacrifice at which these rites were performed: "He who could wholly comprehend this sacrifice could rule the world as though it were spinning on his hand."</apodosis>

Six in the second place means:
<protasis wn_only="rock.n.01, firmness.n.01">Firm as a rock</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="day.n.01, whole.n.02">Not a whole day</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, fortune.n.01">Perseverance brings good fortune</apodosis>.

This describes a person who does not allow himself to be misled by any <apodosis wn_only="illusion.n.01">illusions</apodosis>. While others are letting themselves be dazzled by <apodosis wn_only="enthusiasm.n.01">enthusiasm</apodosis>, he recognizes with perfect <apodosis wn_only="clarity.n.01">clarity</apodosis> the first <apodosis wn_only="sign.n.01, time.n.05">signs of the time</apodosis>. Thus he neither <apodosis wn_only="flattery.n.01">flatters those above</apodosis> him nor <apodosis wn_only="neglect.n.01">neglects those beneath</apodosis> him; he is as <protasis wn_only="rock.n.01, firmness.n.01">firm as a rock</protasis>. When the first <apodosis wn_only="sign.n.01, discord.n.01">sign of discord</apodosis> appears, he knows the right <apodosis wn_only="moment.n.01, withdrawal.n.01">moment for withdrawing</apodosis> and does not <apodosis wn_only="delay.n.01, day.n.01">delay even for a day</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, conduct.n.01, fortune.n.01">Perseverance in such conduct will bring good fortune</apodosis>. Confucius says about this line:

<apodosis wn_only="knowledge.n.01, seed.n.01, divinity.n.01">To know the seeds, that is divine indeed</apodosis>. In his association with those above him, the <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, superiority.n.01, flattery.n.01">superior man does not flatter</apodosis>. In his association with those beneath him, he is not <apodosis wn_only="arrogance.n.01">arrogant</apodosis>. For he <apodosis wn_only="knowledge.n.01, seed.n.01">knows the seeds</apodosis>. The <protasis wn_only="seed.n.01, beginning.n.01, imperceptibility.n.01, movement.n.01">seeds are the first imperceptible beginning of movement</protasis>, the first <apodosis wn_only="trace.n.01, fortune.n.01, misfortune.n.01">trace of good fortune (or misfortune) that shows itself</apodosis>. The <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, superiority.n.01, perception.n.01, seed.n.01, action.n.01">superior man perceives the seeds and immediately takes action</apodosis>. He does not <apodosis wn_only="wait.n.01, day.n.01">wait even a whole day</apodosis>. In the Book of Changes it is said: "<protasis wn_only="rock.n.01, firmness.n.01">Firm as a rock</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="day.n.01, whole.n.02">Not a whole day</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, fortune.n.01">Perseverance brings good fortune</apodosis>."

<protasis wn_only="rock.n.01, firmness.n.01">Firm as a rock</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="need.n.01, day.n.01, whole.n.02">what need of a whole day</apodosis>?

. <apodosis wn_only="judgment.n.01, knowledge.n.01">The judgment can be known</apodosis>.

. <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, superiority.n.01, knowledge.n.01, concealment.n.01, evidence.n.01">The superior man knows what is hidden and what is evident</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="knowledge.n.01, weakness.n.01, strength.n.01">He knows weakness, he knows strength as well</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="myriad.n.01, respect.n.01">Hence the myriads look up to him</apodosis>.

<apodosis wn_only="enthusiasm.n.01, delusion.n.01">Deluded enthusiasm</apodosis>.

<apodosis wn_only="blamelessness.n.01">There is no blame</apodosis>.

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="success.n.03">FOLLOWING has supreme success.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, furtherance.n.02">Perseverance furthers.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="blamelessness.n.01">No blame.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="following.n.02, adaptation.n.02">In order to obtain a following one must first know how to adapt oneself.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="rule.n.01, service.n.01">If a man would rule he must first learn to serve,</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="security.n.01, assent.n.01, following.n.02">for only in this way does he secure from those below him the joyous assent that is necessary if they are to follow him.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="following.n.02, force.n.01, cunning.n.01, conspiracy.n.01, faction.n.01, resistance.n.01, adherence.n.01">If he has to obtain a following by force or cunning, by conspiracy or by creating faction, he invariably arouses resistance, which obstructs willing adherence.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="movement.n.03, consequence.n.01">But even joyous movement can lead to evil consequences,</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="stipulation.n.01, perseverance.n.01, rightness.n.01, blamelessness.n.01">hence the added stipulation, "Perseverance furthers" --that is, consistency in doing right-- together with "No blame."</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="following.n.02, condition.n.01, harm.n.01">Just as we should not ask others to follow us unless this condition is fulfilled, so it is only under this condition that we can in turn follow others without coming to harm.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="thought.n.01, following.n.02, adaptation.n.02, time.n.05, idea.n.01, judgment.n.03">The thought of obtaining a following through adaptation to the demands of the time is a great and significant idea; this is why the appended judgment is so favorable.</apodosis>

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="thunder.n.01, lake.n.01, center.n.01">Thunder in the middle of the lake</protasis>:

THE IMAGE of <apodosis wn_only="following.n.02">FOLLOWING</apodosis>.
Thus the superior man at <protasis wn_only="nightfall.n.01">nightfall</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="home.n.01, rest.n.06, recuperation.n.01">Goes indoors for rest and recuperation</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="autumn.n.01, electricity.n.01, earth.n.01">In the autumn electricity withdraws into the earth again and rests</protasis>. Here it is the <protasis wn_only="thunder.n.01, lake.n.01, center.n.01">thunder in the middle of the lake</protasis> that serves as the image--<protasis wn_only="thunder.n.01, rest.n.06">thunder in its winter rest</protasis>, not <protasis wn_only="thunder.n.01, motion.n.06">thunder in motion</protasis>. The idea of <apodosis wn_only="following.n.02, adaptation.n.02, time.n.05">following in the sense of adaptation to the demands of the time</apodosis> grows out of this image. <protasis wn_only="thunder.n.01, lake.n.01, center.n.01">Thunder in the middle of the lake</protasis> indicates <apodosis wn_only="time.n.05, darkness.n.01, rest.n.06">times of darkness and rest</apodosis>. Similarly, a superior man, after being <protasis wn_only="day.n.04, activity.n.01">tirelessly active all day</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="night.n.01, rest.n.06, recuperation.n.01">allows himself rest and recuperation at night</apodosis>. No situation can become favorable until one is able to <apodosis wn_only="adaptation.n.02">adapt to it</apodosis> and does not <apodosis wn_only="resistance.n.01, error.n.01, exhaustion.n.01">wear himself out with mistaken resistance</apodosis>.

Thus there develops an <apodosis wn_only="tie.n.01, eternity.n.01">eternal tie between the two</apodosis>. The allegory is chosen from the annals of the Chou dynasty. The rulers of this dynasty honored men who had served them well by <apodosis wn_only="award.n.02, place.n.02, temple.n.01, ancestor.n.01, mountain.n.01">awarding them a place in the royal family's temple of ancestors on the Western Mountain</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="corruption.n.06, cause.n.01, knowledge.n.01">We must first know the cause of corruption</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="elimination.n.01">before we can do away with them;</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="caution.n.01, necessity.n.01, time.n.05, start.n.01">hence it is necessary to be cautious during the time before the start</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="way.n.05, safety.n.01, entrance.n.01">Then we must see to it that the new way is safely entered upon,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="relapse.n.01, avoidance.n.01">so that a relapse may be avoided;</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="attention.n.02, time.n.05, start.n.01">therefore we must pay attention to the time after the start</apodosis>.

THE IMAGE

THE LINES
<protasis wn_only="number.n.02">Six in the beginning</protasis> means:

<apodosis wn_only="amends.n.01, wrong.n.02, father.n.01">Setting right what has been spoiled by the father.</apodosis>
<protasis wn_only="son.n.01">If there is a son,</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="blame.n.01, father.n.01, decedent.n.01">No blame rests upon the departed father.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="danger.n.01, fortune.n.03">Danger. In the end good fortune.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="adherence.n.02, tradition.n.01, decay.n.01">Rigid adherence to tradition has resulted in decay.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="decay.n.01, penetration.n.02">But the decay has not yet penetrated deeply</apodosis> and so <apodosis wn_only="remedy.n.01">can still be easily remedied.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="son.n.01, recompense.n.01, decay.n.01, father.n.01">It is as if a son were compensated for the decay his father allowed to creep in.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="blame.n.01, father.n.01">Then no blame attaches to the father.</apodosis> However, <apodosis wn_only="danger.n.01, matter.n.02">one must not overlook the danger or take the matter too lightly.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="consciousness.n.01, danger.n.01, reform.n.02">Only if one is conscious of the danger connected with every reform</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">will everything go well in the end.</apodosis>

Nine in the second place means:
<protasis wn_only="mistake.n.01, weakness.n.01, decay.n.01">Setting right what has been spoiled by the mother.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01">One must not be too persevering.</apodosis>
This refers to <protasis wn_only="error.n.01, weakness.n.01, decay.n.01">mistakes that as a result of weakness have brought about decay</protasis>-hence the symbol, <apodosis wn_only="error.n.01, mother.n.01">"what has been spoiled by the mother."</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="correction.n.01">In setting things right in such a case</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="gentleness.n.01, consideration.n.04">a certain gentle consideration is called for.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="correction.n.01">In order not to wound</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="proceeding.n.01, drasticness.n.01">one should not attempt to proceed too drastically.</apodosis>

Nine in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="correction.n.01, damage.n.01, father.n.01">Setting right what has been spoiled by the father.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="remorse.n.01, blameworthiness.n.01">There will be a little remorse. No great blame.</apodosis>

This describes <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, energy.n.01, correction.n.01, error.n.01, past.n.01">a man who proceeds a little too energetically in righting the mistakes of the past.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="consequence.n.01, discord.n.02, annoyance.n.02">Now and then, as a result, minor discourse and annoyances will surely develop.</apodosis> But <protasis wn_only="energy.n.01">too much energy is better than too little.</protasis> Therefore, although <protasis wn_only="remorse.n.01">he may at times have slight cause for regret,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="blameworthiness.n.01">he remains free of any serious blame.</apodosis>

Six in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="tolerance.n.01, father.n.01, decay.n.01">Tolerating what has been spoiled by the father.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="continuation.n.02, humiliation.n.01">In continuing one sees humiliation.</apodosis>
This shows the situation of someone too weak to take measures against <protasis wn_only="decay.n.01, root.n.01, past.n.01, beginning.n.01, manifestation.n.02">decay that has its roots in the past and is just beginning to manifest itself.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="permission.n.01, course.n.01">It is allowed to run its course.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="continuation.n.02, humiliation.n.01">If this continues, humiliation will result.</apodosis>

Six in the fifth place means:
<protasis wn_only="right.n.01, repair.n.01">Setting right what has been spoiled by the father.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="praise.n.01">One meets with praise.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="person.n.01, confrontation.n.01, corruption.n.04, neglect.n.01">An individual is confronted with corruption originating from neglect in former times.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="power.n.01, ward.n.02, helper.n.03, reform.n.02">He lacks the power to ward it off alone, but with able helpers he can at least bring about a thorough reform, if he cannot create a new beginning, and this also is praiseworthy.</apodosis>


Nine at the top means:

<protasis wn_only="service.n.01, king.n.01, prince.n.01">He does not serve kings and princes,</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="goal.n.01">Sets himself higher goals.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, obligation.n.01, affair.n.01, world.n.08">Not every man has an obligation to mingle in the affairs of the world.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="development.n.01, justification.n.01, world.n.08">There are some who are developed to such a degree that they are justified in letting the world go its own way and refusing to enter public life with a view to reforming it.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="right.n.01, idleness.n.01, criticism.n.01">But this does not imply a right to remain idle or to sit back and merely criticize.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="withdrawal.n.01, justification.n.01, realization.n.04, goal.n.01, mankind.n.01">Such withdrawal is justified only when we strive to realize in ourselves the higher aims of mankind.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="sage.n.01, distance.n.01, life.n.01, creation.n.02, value.n.01, future.n.01">For although the sage remains distant from the turmoil of daily life, he creates incomparable human values for the future.</apodosis>

<token id="kuan">
<protasis wn_only="stress.n.01, name.n.01, meaning.n.01">A slight variation of tonal stress gives the Chinese name for this hexagram a double meaning.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, exemplar.n.01">It means both contemplating and being seen, in the sense of being an example.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="idea.n.01, fact.n.01, hexagram.n.01, tower.n.01, china.n.01">These ideas are suggested by the fact that the hexagram can be understood as picturing a type of tower characteristic of ancient China.</protasis>

<protasis wn_only="tower.n.01, view.n.02, country.n.04">A tower of this kind commanded a wide view of the country;</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="mountain.n.01, landmark.n.01">at the same time, when situated on a mountain, it became a landmark that could be seen for miles around.</apodosis>

<apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, ruler.n.01, law.n.01, heaven.n.01, people.n.01, government.n.01, example.n.01, mass.n.01">Thus the hexagram shows a ruler who contemplates the law of heaven above him and the ways of the people below, and who, by means of good government, sets a lofty example to the masses.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, month.n.01">This hexagram is linked with the eight month (September-October).</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="power.n.01, increase.n.01">The light-giving power retreats and the dark power is again on the increase.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="aspect.n.02, interpretation.n.01, hexagram.n.01">However, this aspect is not material in the interpretation of the hexagram as a whole.</apodosis>

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="ablution.n.01">The ablution has been made</protasis>,
But <apodosis wn_only="offering.n.01">not yet the offering</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="trust.n.01">Full of trust</apodosis> they <protasis wn_only="look.n.01">look up to him</protasis>.

The <protasis wn_only="sacrifice.n.01, ritual.n.01">sacrificial ritual in China</protasis> <protasis wn_only="begin.v.01, ablution.n.01, libation.n.01">began with an ablution and a libation</protasis> by which <apodosis wn_only="deity.n.01">the Deity was invoked</apodosis>, after which <apodosis wn_only="sacrifice.n.01">the sacrifice was offered</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="moment.n.01, time.n.05">The moment of time</protasis> between these two ceremonies is <apodosis wn_only="sacred.a.01">the most sacred of all</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="moment.n.01, concentration.n.02">the moment of deepest inner concentration</apodosis>. If <protasis wn_only="piety.n.01, sincerity.n.01, faith.n.01">piety is sincere and expressive of real faith</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, transformation.n.02, awe.n.01">the contemplation of it has a transforming awe-spiring effect</apodosis> on those who witness it. Thus also in nature <apodosis wn_only="seriousness.n.01">a holy seriousness</apodosis> is to be seen in the fact that <protasis wn_only="natural_phenomenon.n.01, law.n.01">natural occurrences are uniformly subject to law</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, meaning.n.02">Contemplation of the divine meaning</protasis> underlying <protasis wn_only="universe.n.01">the workings of the universe</protasis> gives to the man who is called upon to influence others <apodosis wn_only="means.n.01, production.n.01, effect.n.01">the means of producing like effects</apodosis>. This requires that <protasis wn_only="power.n.01, concentration.n.02">power of inner concentration</protasis> which <apodosis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, development.n.01">religious contemplation develops</apodosis> in <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, faith.n.01">great men strong in faith</protasis>. It enables them to <apodosis wn_only="apprehension.n.02, law.n.01">apprehend the mysterious and divine laws of life</apodosis>, and by means of <protasis wn_only="concentration.n.02">profoundest inner concentration</protasis> they <apodosis wn_only="expression.n.02, law.n.01, person.n.01">give expression to these laws in their own persons</apodosis>. Thus <apodosis wn_only="power.n.01, emanation.n.02">a hidden spiritual power emanates from them</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="influence.n.01, domination.n.02">influencing and dominating others</apodosis> without their being aware of how it happens.

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="wind.n.01, earth.n.01">The wind blows over the earth</protasis>:
<apodosis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, image.n.01">The image of CONTEMPLATION</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="king.n.01, past.n.01, world.n.08, region.n.01, visit.n.01">Thus the kings of old visited the regions of the world</apodosis>,

THE LINES

<apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, superiority.n.01, humiliation.n.01">For a superior man, humiliation.</apodosis>

This means <apodosis wn_only="contemplation.n.01, distance.n.01, comprehension.n.01">contemplation from a distance, without comprehension.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, influence.n.01">A man of influence is at hand,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="influence.n.01, understanding.n.01, people.n.01">abut his influence is not understood by the common people.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="importance.n.01, people.n.01, mass.n.03, benefit.n.01, action.n.01, sage.n.01, understanding.n.01">This matters little in the case of the masses, for they benefit by the actions of the ruling sage whether they understand them or not.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, superiority.n.01, disgrace.n.01">But for a superior man it is a disgrace.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="contentment.n.01, view.n.01, shallowness.n.01, thoughtlessness.n.01, force.n.01">He must not content himself with a shallow, thoughtless view of prevailing forces;</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="contemplation.n.01, whole.n.02, connection.n.01, understanding.n.01">he must contemplate them as a connected whole and try to understand them.</apodosis>

Six in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, life.n.06">Contemplation of my life</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="choice.n.02, advance.n.01, retreat.n.01">Decides the choice
Between advance and retreat.</apodosis>

This is the place of <apodosis wn_only="transition.n.01">transition</apodosis>. We no longer <protasis wn_only="appearance.n.02">look outward to receive pictures that are more or less limited and confused</protasis>, but <apodosis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, self.n.01">direct out contemplation upon ourselves</apodosis> in order to <apodosis wn_only="guideline.n.01, decision.n.01">find a guideline for our decisions</apodosis>. This <protasis wn_only="self-contemplation.n.01">self-contemplation</protasis> means the <apodosis wn_only="overcoming.n.02, egotism.n.01, naivete.n.01">overcoming of naive egotism</apodosis> in the <protasis wn_only="person.n.01, standpoint.n.01">person who sees everything solely form his own standpoint</protasis>. He begins to <apodosis wn_only="reflection.n.01, objectivity.n.01">reflect and in this way acquires objectivity</apodosis>. However, <protasis wn_only="self-knowledge.n.01, preoccupation.n.01, thought.n.01">self-knowledge does not mean preoccupation with one's own thoughts</protasis>; rather, it means <apodosis wn_only="concern.n.01, effect.n.01">concern about the effects one creates</apodosis>. It is only the <protasis wn_only="effect.n.01, life.n.06">effects our lives produce</protasis> that <apodosis wn_only="right.n.01, judgment.n.03, progress.n.01, regression.n.01">give us the right to judge whether what we have done means progress or regression</apodosis>.

Six in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, light.n.02, kingdom.n.01">Contemplation of the light of the kingdom.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="influence.n.01, guest.n.01, king.n.01">It furthers one to exert influence as the guest of a king.</apodosis>

This describes a man who understands the secrets by which a kingdom can be made to flourish. Such a man must be given an authoritative position, in which he can exert influence. He should be, so to speak, a guest-that is, he should be honored and act independently, and should not be used as a tool.

Nine at the top means:

<protasis wn_only="contemplation.n.02, life.n.01">Contemplation of his life.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, blamelessness.n.01">The superior man is without blame.</apodosis>

While the preceding line represents a man who contemplates himself, here in the highest place everything that is personal, related to the ego, is excluded. The picture is that of a sage who stands outside the affairs of the world. Liberated from his ego, he contemplates the laws of life and so realizes that knowing how to become free of blame is the highest good.
</token>

Nine in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="ridgepole.n.01, sag.n.01, break.n.01, point.n.01">The ridgepole sags to the breaking point.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="misfortune.n.01">Misfortune.</apodosis>
This indicates a type of man who in times of preponderance of the great insists on pushing ahead. He accepts no advice from others, and therefore they in turn are not willing to lend him support. Because of this the burden grows, until <apodosis wn_only="structure.n.01, break.n.01">the structure of things bends or breaks.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="plunge.n.01, time.n.05, danger.n.01, catastrophe.n.01">Plunging willfully ahead in times of danger only hastens the catastrophe.</apodosis>

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="dark.n.01, light.n.02">What is dark clings to what is light</protasis> and so <apodosis wn_only="brightness.n.01, enhancement.n.01">enhances the brightness of the latter</apodosis>.

Thus <protasis wn_only="sun.n.01, moon.n.01, heaven.n.01">the sun and moon cling to heaven</protasis>, and <protasis wn_only="grain.n.01, grass.n.01, tree.n.01, earth.n.01">grain, grass, and trees cling to the earth</protasis>.

Nine in the second place means:
<protasis wn_only="perseverance.n.01">Perseverance</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">good fortune</apodosis>.

The premise here is that <protasis wn_only="gate.n.01, success.n.01">the gates to success</protasis> are beginning to <apodosis wn_only="opening.n.01">open</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="resistance.n.01">Resistance</protasis> gives way and <apodosis wn_only="forge.v.02">we forge ahead</apodosis>. This is the point at which, only too easily, <protasis wn_only="prey.n.01, self-confidence.n.01">we become the prey of exuberant self-confidence</protasis>. This is why the oracle says that <protasis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, equilibrium.n.01">perseverance (i.e., perseverance in inner equilibrium, without excessive use of power)</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">good fortune</apodosis>.

Nine in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, inferior.n.01">The inferior man</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="work.n.01, power.n.01">works through power</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, superior.n.01">The superior man</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="act.n.02">does not act thus</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="continuation.n.02">To continue</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="danger.n.01">is dangerous</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="goat.n.01, butt.n.02, hedge.n.01">A goat butts against a hedge</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="horn.n.02, entanglement.n.01">And gets its horns entangled</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="boast.n.01, power.n.01">Making a boast of power</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="entanglement.n.01">leads to entanglements</apodosis>, <protasis wn_only="goat.n.01, horn.n.02, entanglement.n.01, butt.n.02, hedge.n.01">just as a goat entangles its horns when it butts against a hedge</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, inferior.n.01, power.n.01, possession.n.01">Whereas an inferior man revels in power when he comes into possession of it</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, superior.n.01, mistake.n.01">the superior man never makes this mistake</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="consciousness.n.01, danger.n.01, pushing.n.01, circumstance.n.01">He is conscious at all times of the danger of pushing ahead regardless of circumstances</protasis>, and therefore <apodosis wn_only="renunciation.n.01, display.n.01, force.n.01">renounces in good time the empty display of force</apodosis>.

Nine in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="perseverance.n.01">Perseverance</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">good fortune</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="remorse.n.01, disappearance.n.01">Remorse disappears</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="hedge.n.01, opening.n.01">The hedge opens</protasis>; <apodosis wn_only="entanglement.n.01">there is no entanglement</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="power.n.01, dependence.n.01, axle.n.01, cart.n.01">Power depends upon the axle of a big cart</protasis>.

If <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, work.n.01, removal.n.01, resistance.n.01">a man goes on quietly and perseveringly working at the removal of resistances</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="success.n.01">success comes in the end</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="obstruction.n.01, way.n.04">The obstructions give way</apodosis> and <apodosis wn_only="occasion.n.01, remorse.n.01, use.n.01, power.n.01, disappearance.n.01">all occasion for remorse arising from excessive use of power disappears</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, power.n.01">Such a man's power does not show externally</protasis>, yet <apodosis wn_only="load.n.01, cart.n.01, strength.n.01, axle.n.01">it can move heavy loads, like a big cart whose real strength lies in its axle</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="power.n.01, application.n.02">The less that power is applied outwardly</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="effect.n.01">the greater its effect</apodosis>.
