THE LINES

Six at the beginning means:
<protasis wn_only="travel.n.01, barrier.n.01">Going leads to obstructions</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="arrival.n.01, praise.n.01">Coming meets with praise</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="obstruction.n.01, encounter.n.01">When one encounters an obstruction</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="reflection.n.01, importance.n.01">the important thing is to reflect on how best to deal with it</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="danger.n.01, threat.n.01">When threatened with danger</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="blindness.n.02, endeavor.n.01">one should not strive blindly to go ahead</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="complexity.n.01">for this only leads to complications</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="correctness.n.01, retreat.n.01">The correct thing is, on the contrary, to retreat for the time being</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="surrender.n.01">not in order to give up the struggle</apodosis> but <apodosis wn_only="wait.n.01, moment.n.01, action.n.01">to await the right moment for action</apodosis>.

Six in the second place means:
<protasis wn_only="king.n.01, servant.n.01, obstruction.n.01">The King's servant is beset by obstruction upon obstruction</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="fault.n.01">But it is not his own fault</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="obstacle.n.01, resistance.n.01">Ordinarily it is best to go around an obstacle and try to overcome it along the line of least resistance</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="instance.n.01, man.n.01, trouble.n.01, difficulty.n.01">But there is one instance in which a man must go out to meet the trouble, even though difficulty piles upon difficulty</apodosis>: <protasis wn_only="path.n.02, duty.n.01, danger.n.01">this is when the path of duty leads directly to it-in other words, when he cannot act of his own volition but is duty bound to go and seek out danger in the service of a higher cause</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="compunction.n.01, fault.n.01, situation.n.01">Then he may do it without compunction, because it is not through any fault of his that he is putting himself in this difficult situation</apodosis>.

Nine in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="travel.n.01, obstruction.n.01">Going leads to obstructions</protasis>;
<apodosis wn_only="return.n.01">Hence he comes back</apodosis>.

While the preceding line shows the official compelled by duty to follow the way of danger, this line shows the man who must act as <apodosis wn_only="father.n.01, family.n.01, head.n.01, kinship.n.01">father of a family or as head of his kin</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="plunge.n.01, danger.n.01, recklessness.n.01, uselessness.n.01">If he were to plunge recklessly in to danger, it would be a useless act</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="trust.n.01, care.n.01">because those entrusted to his care cannot get along by themselves</apodosis>. But <protasis wn_only="withdrawal.n.01, return.n.01">if he withdraws and turns back to his own</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="welcome.n.01, joy.n.01">they welcome him with great joy</apodosis>.

Six in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="travel.n.01, obstruction.n.02">Going leads to obstructions</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="arrival.n.01, union.n.05">Coming leads to union</apodosis>.

This too describes <protasis wn_only="situation.n.01, management.n.02">a situation that cannot be managed single-handed</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="case.n.01, path.n.03, shortness.n.01">In such a case the direct way is not the shortest</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="person.n.01, strength.n.01, preparation.n.02">If a person were to forge ahead on his own strength and without the necessary preparations</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="support.n.01, realization.n.02, mistake.n.01, calculation.n.01">he would not find the support he needs and would realize too late that he has been mistaken in his calculations</apodosis>, <protasis wn_only="condition.n.01, reliance.n.02">inasmuch as the conditions on which he hoped he could rely</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="inadequacy.n.01">would prove to be inadequate</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="case.n.01, holding.n.02, time.n.05, gathering.n.01, companion.n.03, trust.n.01, help.n.01, overcoming.n.02, obstruction.n.02">In this case it is better, therefore, to hold back for the time being and to gather together trustworthy companions who can be counted upon for help in overcoming the obstructions</apodosis>.

Nine in the fifth place means:
<protasis wn_only="obstruction.n.02">In the midst of the greatest obstructions</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="friend.n.01, arrival.n.01">Friends come</apodosis>.

Here we see a man who is called to help in an emergency. He should not seek to evade the obstructions, no matter how dangerously they pile up before him. But because he is really called to the task, the power of his spirit is strong enough to attract helpers whom he can effectively organize, so that through the well-directed co-operation of all participants the obstruction is overcome.


Six at the top means:

<protasis wn_only="travel.n.01, obstruction.n.02">Going leads to obstructions</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="arrival.n.01, fortune.n.03">Coming leads to great good fortune</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="benefit.n.01, man.n.01">It furthers one to see the great man</apodosis>.

This refers to a man who has already left the world and its tumult behind him. When the time of obstructions arrives, it might seem that the simplest thing for him to do would be to turn his back upon the world and take refuge in the beyond. But this road is barred to him. He must not seek his own salvation and abandon the world to its adversity. Duty calls him back once more into the turmoil of life. Precisely because of his experience and inner freedom, he is able to create something both great and complete that brings good fortune. And it is favorable to see the great man in alliance with whom one can achieve the work of rescue.
</token>

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, burden.n.01, back.n.01">If a man carries a burden on his back</protasis>

Confucius says about this line:

<protasis wn_only="burden.n.01, back.n.01, business.n.01, man.n.01">Carrying a burden on the back is the business of common man</protasis>; <protasis wn_only="carriage.n.02, appurtenance.n.01, man.n.01, rank.n.01">a carriage is the appurtenance of a man of rank</protasis>. Now, <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, appurtenance.n.01, man.n.01, rank.n.01">when a common man uses the appurtenance of man of rank</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="robber.n.01, plot.n.01">robbers plot to take it away from him</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, insolence.n.01">If a man is insolent toward those above him</protasis> and <protasis wn_only="hardness.n.01">hard toward those below him</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="robber.n.01, plot.n.01, attack.n.01">robbers plot to attack him</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="carelessness.n.01, guard.v.01, thing.n.01, temptation.n.01, thief.n.01, steal.v.01">Carelessness in guarding things tempts thieves to steal</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="sumptuousness.n.01, ornament.n.01, maiden.n.01, enticement.n.01, robbery.n.01, virtue.n.01">Sumptuous ornaments worn by a maiden are an enticement to rob her of her virtue</apodosis>.

Nine in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="liberation.n.01, toe.n.01">Deliver yourself from your great toe.</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="heap.n.01, thing.n.12, smallness.n.01, order.n.01, achievement.n.01, highness.n.01, greatness.n.01">Heaps up small things

<protasis wn_only="adaptation.n.01, obstacle.n.01, wood.n.01, earth.n.01, growth.n.01, upward.n.01, haste.n.01, rest.n.01">Adapting itself to obstacles and bending around them, wood in the earth grows upward without haste and without rest.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, character.n.01, devotion.n.01, progress.n.01, pause.n.01">Thus too the superior man is devoted in character and never pauses in his progress.</apodosis>

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="town.n.01, change.n.01">The town may be changed</protasis>,
<apodosis wn_only="well.n.01, change.n.01">But the well cannot be changed</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="decrease.n.01, increase.n.01">It neither decreases nor increases</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="people.n.01, come.v.01, go.v.01, draw.v.01, well.n.01">They come and go and draw from the well</protasis>.
<protasis wn_only="person.n.01, get.v.01, water.n.06, rope.n.01, go.v.01">If one gets down almost to the water
And the rope does not go all the way</protasis>,
<protasis wn_only="jug.n.01, break.v.01">Or the jug breaks</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="misfortune.n.01">it brings misfortune</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="china.n.01, capital.n.01, city.n.01, move.v.01, location.n.01, change.n.01, dynasty.n.01">In ancient China the capital cities were sometimes moved, partly for the sake of more favorable location, partly because of a change in dynasties</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="architecture.n.01, style.n.01, change.v.01, century.n.01">The style of architecture changed in the course of centuries</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="well.n.01, shape.n.02, remain.v.01, time.n.05">but the shape of the well has remained the same from ancient times to this day</apodosis>. <apodosis <token id="ting">
<protasis wn_only="line.n.01, image.n.01, caldron.n.01">The six lines construct the image of Ting, THE CALDRON</protasis>; <apodosis wn_only="leg.n.01, bottom.n.01">at the bottom are the legs</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="belly.n.01">over them the belly</apodosis>, then come <apodosis wn_only="ear.n.01, handle.n.01">the ears (handles)</apodosis>, and <apodosis wn_only="ring.n.01, top.n.01">at the top the carrying rings</apodosis>. At the same time, <protasis wn_only="image.n.01, suggestion.n.01, idea.n.01, nourishment.n.01">the image suggests the idea of nourishment</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="ting.n.01, bronze.n.01, vessel.n.01, food.n.01, temple.n.01, ancestor.n.01, banquet.n.01">The ting, cast of bronze, was the vessel that held the cooked viands in the temple of the ancestors and at banquets.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="head.n.01, family.n.01, food.n.01, ting.n.01, bowl.n.01, guest.n.01">The heads of the family served the food from the ting into the bowls of the guests.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="well.n.01, meaning.n.01, nourishment.n.01, people.n.01">THE WELL 48 likewise has the secondary meaning of giving nourishment, but rather more in relation to the people.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="ting.n.01, utensil.n.01, civilization.n.01, suggestion.n.01, man.n.01, state.n.01">The ting, as a utensil pertaining to a refined civilization, suggests the fostering and nourishing of able men, which redounded to the benefit of the state.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, well.n.01, book_of_changes.n.01, object.n.01">This hexagram and THE WELL are the only two in the Book of Changes that represent concrete, men-made objects.</apodosis> Yet here too <protasis wn_only="thought.n.01, connotation.n.01">the thought has its abstract connotation</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="sun.n.01, wood.n.01, wind.n.01, li.n.01, flame.n.01">Sun, below, is wood and wind; Li, above, is flame.</protasis> Thus together <apodosis wn_only="flame.n.01, wood.n.01, wind.n.01, suggestion.n.01, idea.n.01, food.n.01">they stand for the flame kindled by wood and wind, which likewise suggests the idea of preparing food</apodosis>.

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="caldron.n.01">THE CALDRON</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.01">Supreme good fortune</apodosis>.

<apodosis wn_only="success.n.01">Success</apodosis>.

While <protasis wn_only="well.n.01">THE WELL</protasis> relates to <apodosis wn_only="foundation.n.01, life.n.01">the social foundation of our life</apodosis>, and <protasis wn_only="foundation.n.01, water.n.01, wood.n.01">this foundation is likened to the water that serves to nourish growing wood</protasis>, <protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01">the present hexagram</protasis> refers to <apodosis wn_only="superstructure.n.01, society.n.01">the cultural superstructure of society</apodosis>. Here <protasis wn_only="wood.n.01, flame.n.01, spirit.n.01">it is the wood that serves as nourishment for the flame, the spirit</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="entity.n.01, realm.n.02">All that is visible must grow beyond itself, extend into the realm of the invisible</protasis>. Thereby <apodosis wn_only="consecration.n.01, clarity.n.01, order.n.01">it receives its true consecration and clarity and takes firm root in the cosmic order</apodosis>. Here we see <apodosis wn_only="civilization.n.01, religion.n.01">civilization as it reaches its culmination in religion</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="ting.n.01, sacrifice.n.01, god.n.01">The ting serves in offering sacrifice to God</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="value.n.01, god.n.01">The highest earthly values must be sacrificed to the divine</apodosis>. But <protasis wn_only="god.n.01, man.n.01">the truly divine does not manifest itself apart from man</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="revelation.n.02, god.n.01, prophet.n.01, man.n.01">The supreme revelation of God appears in prophets and holy men</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="veneration.n.01, god.n.01">To venerate them is true veneration of God</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="will.n.01, god.n.01, humility.n.01">The will of God, as revealed through them, should be accepted in humility</protasis>; <apodosis wn_only="enlightenment.n.02, understanding.n.01, world.n.01">this brings inner enlightenment and true understanding of the world</apodosis>, and <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.01, success.n.01">this leads to great good fortune and success</apodosis>.

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="fire.n.01, wood.n.01">Fire over wood</protasis>:

<apodosis wn_only="image.n.01, caldron.n.01">The image of THE CALDRON.</apodosis>

<apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, fate.n.01, position.n.01">Thus the superior man consolidates his fate
By making his position correct.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="fate.n.01, fire.n.01, wood.n.01">The fate of fire depends on wood; as long as there is wood below, the fire burns above.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="life.n.01, man.n.01, fate.n.01, power.n.01">It is the same in human life; there is in man likewise a fate that lends power to his life.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="fate.n.01, life.n.01, harmony.n.03">And if he succeeds in assigning the right place to life and to fate, thus bringing the two into harmony, he puts his fate on a firm footing.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="word.n.01, hint.n.01, life.n.01, tradition.n.01, teaching.n.01, yoga.n.01">These words contain hints about fostering of life as handed on by oral tradition in the secret teachings of Chinese yoga.</apodosis>

THE LINES

<protasis wn_only="ting.n.01, leg.n.01, position.n.01">A ting with legs upturned.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="removal.n.01, stagnation.n.01, stuff.n.01">Furthers removal of stagnating stuff.</apodosis>

<apodosis wn_only="blameworthiness.n.01">No blame.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="ting.n.01, position.n.01, use.n.01">If a ting is turned upside down before being used,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="harm.n.01">no harm is done</apodosis>-<apodosis wn_only="refuse.n.01, clearance.n.01">on the contrary, this clears it of refuse.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="concubine.n.01, position.n.01, lowliness.n.01, son.n.01">A concubine's position is lowly, but because she has a son</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="honor.n.01">she comes to be honored.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="metaphor.n.01, idea.n.01, civilization.n.01, development.n.01, hexagram.n.01, person.n.01, goodwill.n.01, success.n.01">These two metaphors express the idea that in a highly developed civilization, such as that indicated by this hexagram, every person of good will can in some way or other succeed.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="lowliness.n.01, readiness.n.01, purification.n.01">No matter how lowly he may be, provided he is ready to purify himself,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="acceptance.n.01">he is accepted.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="station.n.01, attainment.n.01, fruitfulness.n.01, accomplishment.n.01, recognition.n.01">He attains a station in which he can prove himself fruitful in accomplishment, and as a result he gains recognition.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="leg.n.03, tripod.n.01, break.n.01">The legs of the ting are broken.</protasis>

<token id="chen">
<protasis wn_only="yang.n.01, line.n.01, yin.n.01, line.n.01, force.n.01, upward.n.01">A yang line develops below two yin lines and presses upward forcibly.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="movement.n.01, violence.n.01, terror.n.01">This movement is so violent that it arouses terror.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="thunder.n.01, earth.n.01, shock.n.01, fear.n.01, trembling.n.01">It is symbolized by thunder, which bursts forth from the earth and by its shock causes fear and trembling.</apodosis>

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01">SHOCK</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="success.n.01">success</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01">Shock</protasis> comes-oh, oh!
<apodosis wn_only="laughter.n.01, word.n.01">Laughing words</apodosis> -ha, ha!

<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, panic.n.01, mile.n.01">The shock terrifies for a hundred miles</protasis>,
And <apodosis wn_only="male.n.01, sacrifice.n.01, spoon.n.01, chalice.n.01">he does not let fall the sacrificial spoon and chalice</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, manifestation.n.01, god.n.01, depth.n.01, earth.n.01, fear.n.01">The shock that comes from the manifestation of God within the depths of the earth makes man afraid</protasis>, but <apodosis wn_only="fear.n.01, god.n.01, good.n.01, joy.n.01, merriment.n.01">this fear of God is good, for joy and merriment can follow upon it</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="male.n.01, learning.n.01, heart.n.01, fear.n.01, trembling.n.01">When a man has learned within his heart what fear and trembling mean</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="protection.n.01, terror.n.01, influence.n.01">he is safeguarded against any terror produced by outside influences</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="thunder.n.01, terror.n.01, mile.n.01">Let the thunder roll and spread terror a hundred miles around</protasis>: <apodosis wn_only="male.n.01, composure.n.01, reverence.n.01, spirit.n.01, sacrifice.n.01, rite.n.01">he remains so composed and reverent in spirit that the sacrificial rite is not interrupted</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="spirit.n.01, leader.n.01, ruler.n.01, male.n.01">This is the spirit that must animate leaders and rulers of men</protasis>-<apodosis wn_only="seriousness.n.01, terror.n.01">a profound inner seriousness from which all terrors glance off harmlessly</apodosis>.

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="thunder.n.01, repetition.n.01">Thunder repeated</protasis>: <apodosis wn_only="image.n.01, shock.n.01">the image of SHOCK</apodosis>.

Thus <apodosis wn_only="fear.n.01, trembling.n.01">in fear and trembling</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, superior.n.01">The superior man</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="life.n.01, order.n.01">sets his life in order</apodosis>
And <apodosis wn_only="examination.n.01">examines himself</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, thunder.n.01, continuity.n.01">The shock of continuing thunder</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="fear.n.01, trembling.n.01">brings fear and trembling</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="man.n.01, superior.n.01">The superior man</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="reverence.n.01, manifestation.n.01, god.n.01">is always filled with reverence at the manifestation of God</apodosis>; <apodosis wn_only="life.n.01, order.n.01">he sets his life in order</apodosis> and <apodosis wn_only="heart.n.01, search.n.01">searches his heart</apodosis>, <apodosis wn_only="opposition.n.01, will.n.01, god.n.01">lest it harbor any secret opposition to the will of God</apodosis>. Thus <apodosis wn_only="reverence.n.01, foundation.n.01, culture.n.01">reverence is the foundation of true culture</apodosis>.

THE LINES

Nine at the beginning means:
<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01">Shock comes-oh, oh!</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="word.n.01, laughter.n.01">Then follow laughing words-ha, ha!</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">Good fortune.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="fear.n.01, trembling.n.01, shock.n.01">The fear and trembling engendered by shock</protasis> come to an individual at first in such a way that <apodosis wn_only="disadvantage.n.01, person.n.01, other.n.01">he sees himself placed at a disadvantage as against others</apodosis>. But <protasis wn_only="transitory.n.01">this is only transitory</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="ordeal.n.01">When the ordeal is over</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="relief.n.01">he experiences relief</apodosis>, and thus <apodosis wn_only="terror.n.01, fortune.n.03">the very terror he had to endure at the outset brings good fortune in the long run</apodosis>.

Six in the second place means:
<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, danger.n.01">Shock comes bringing danger.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="time.n.05">A hundred thousand times</apodosis>
<protasis wn_only="loss.n.01, treasure.n.01">You lose your treasures</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="climb.n.01, hill.n.01">And must climb the nine hills.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="pursuit.n.01">Do not go in pursuit of them.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="day.n.01, return.n.01">After seven days you will get them back again.</apodosis>

This pictures a situation in which <protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, danger.n.01, man.n.01, suffering.n.01, loss.n.01">a shock endangers a man and he suffers great losses.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="resistance.n.01, time.n.05, movement.n.03, success.n.01">Resistance would be contrary to the movement of the time and for this reason unsuccessful.</apodosis> Therefore <apodosis wn_only="retreat.n.01, height.n.01, force.n.01, danger.n.01">he must simply retreat to heights inaccessible to the threatening forces of danger.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="acceptance.n.02, loss.n.01, property.n.01, worry.n.01">He must accept his loss of property without worrying too much about it.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="time.n.05, shock.n.01, upheaval.n.01, robbery.n.01, possession.n.01, return.n.01, pursuit.n.01">When the time of shock and upheaval that has robbed him of his possessions has passed, he will get them back again without going in pursuit of them.</apodosis>

Six in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01">Shock comes</protasis> and <apodosis wn_only="distress.n.01">makes one distraught</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, action.n.01">If shock spurs to action</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="freedom.n.01, misfortune.n.01">One remains free of misfortune</apodosis>.
There are three kinds of shock-<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, heaven.n.01, thunder.n.01">the shock of heaven, which is thunder</protasis>, <protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, fate.n.01">the shock of fate</protasis>, and, finally, <protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, heart.n.01">the shock of the heart</protasis>. The present hexagram refers less to <protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, heart.n.01">inner shock</protasis> than to <protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, fate.n.01">the shock of fate</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="time.n.05, shock.n.01">In such times of shock</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="presence_of_mind.n.01">presence of mind is all too easily lost</apodosis>: <apodosis wn_only="individual.n.01, opportunity.n.01, action.n.01">the individual overlooks all opportunities for action</apodosis> and <apodosis wn_only="fate.n.01">mutely lets fate take its course</apodosis>. But <protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, fate.n.01, movement.n.03, mind.n.01">if he allows the shocks of fate to induce movement within his mind</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="blow.n.05, effort.n.01">he will overcome these external blows with little effort</apodosis>.

Nine in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, mire.n.01">Shock is mired.</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="travel.n.01, mind.n.01, success.n.03, circumstance.n.01">Movement within the mind depends for its success partly on circumstances.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="resistance.n.01, combat.n.01, surrender.n.01, permission.n.01, victory.n.01">If there is neither a resistance that might be vigorously combated, nor yet a yielding that permits of victory</protasis>-<protasis wn_only="mire.n.01, toughness.n.01, inertia.n.01">if, instead, everything is tough and inert like mire</protasis>-<apodosis wn_only="travel.n.01, cripple.n.01">movement is crippled</apodosis>.

Six in the fifth place means:
<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, movement.n.03">Shock goes hither and thither.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="danger.n.01">Danger.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="loss.n.01">However, nothing at all is lost.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="task.n.01">Yet there are things to be done.</apodosis>

This is a case not of a single shock but of <protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, repetition.n.01, space.n.01">repeated shocks with no breathing space between</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="shock.n.01, loss.n.01">Nonetheless, the shock causes no loss</apodosis>, because <protasis wn_only="care.n.01, center.n.01, movement.n.03">one takes care to stay in the center of movement</protasis> and <apodosis wn_only="fate.n.01">in this way to be spared the fate of being helplessly tossed hither and thither</apodosis>.


Six at the top means:

<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, ruin.n.01, terror.n.01, gaze.n.01">Shock brings ruin and terrified gazing around.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="progress.n.01, misfortune.n.01">Going ahead brings misfortune.</apodosis>
<protasis wn_only="body.n.01, neighbor.n.01">If it has not yet touched one's own body
But has reached one's neighbor first,</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="blame.n.01">There is no blame.</apodosis>
<apodosis wn_only="comrade.n.01, conversation.n.01">One's comrades have something to talk about.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="shock.n.01, height.n.01, reflection.n.01, clarity.n.01, vision.n.01">When inner shock is at its height, it robs a man of reflection and clarity of vision.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="shock.n.01, impossibility.n.01, action.n.01, presence_of_mind.n.01">In such a state of shock it is of course impossible to act with presence of mind.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="withdrawal.n.01, composure.n.01, clarity.n.01">Then the right thing is to keep still until composure and clarity are restored.</apodosis> But <protasis wn_only="infection.n.01, agitation.n.01, visibility.n.01, effect.n.01">this a man can do only when he himself is not yet infected by the agitation, although its disastrous effects are already visible in those around him.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="withdrawal.n.01, time.n.05, freedom.n.01, mistake.n.01, injury.n.01">If he withdraws from the affair in time, he remains free of mistakes and injury.</apodosis> But <protasis wn_only="comrade.n.01, warning.n.01, excitement.n.01, displeasure.n.01">his comrades, who no longer heed any warning, will in their excitement certainly be displeased with him.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="account.n.07">However, he must not take this into account.</apodosis>

In this case <protasis wn_only="attempt.n.01, penetration.n.02, domain.n.02">any attempt to penetrate into the personal domain of darkness</protasis> would only <apodosis wn_only="harm.n.01">bring harm</apodosis>.
</token>

<token id="tui">
<protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, sun.n.01, trigram.n.01">This hexagram, like sun, is one of the eight formed by doubling of a trigram.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="trigram.n.01, daughter.n.01, lake.n.01, joy.n.01">The trigram Tui denotes the youngest daughter; it is symbolized by the smiling lake, and its attribute is joyousness.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="appearance.n.01, quality.n.01, line.n.04, joy.n.01">Contrary to appearances, it is not the yielding quality of the top line that accounts for joy here.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="attribute.n.02, principle.n.01, melancholy.n.01">The attribute of the yielding or dark principle is not joy but melancholy.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="joy.n.01, line.n.04, strength.n.01, gentleness.n.01">However, joy is indicated by the fact that there are two strong lines within, expressing themselves through the medium of gentleness.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="joy.n.01, firmness.n.02, strength.n.01, gentleness.n.01">True joy, therefore, rests on firmness and strength within, manifesting itself outwardly as yielding and gentle.</apodosis>

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="joy.n.01,mood.n.01">The joyous mood</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="contagion.n.01,success.n.01">is infectious and therefore brings success</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="joy.n.01,steadfastness.n.01">But joy must be based on steadfastness</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="degeneracy.n.02,mirth.n.01">if it is not to degenerate into uncontrolled mirth</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="truth.n.01,strength.n.01,heart.n.01">Truth and strength must dwell in the heart</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="gentleness.n.01,intercourse.n.01">while gentleness reveals itself in social intercourse</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="attitude.n.01,god.n.01,man.n.01">In this way one assumes the right attitude toward God and man</protasis> and <apodosis wn_only="achievement.n.01">achieves something</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="intimidation.n.01">Under certain conditions, intimidation without gentleness</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="achievement.n.01,moment.n.01,time.n.05">may achieve something momentarily, but not for all time</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="heart.n.01,man.n.01,friendliness.n.01">When, on the other hand, the hearts of men are won by friendliness</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="hardship.n.01,death.n.01,power.n.01,joy.n.01,man.n.01">they are led to take all hardships upon themselves willingly, and if need be will not shun death itself, so great is the power of joy over men</apodosis>.

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="lake.n.01, image.n.01">Lakes resting one on the other: The image of THE JOYOUS.</protasis>

<apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, friend.n.01, discussion.n.02, practice.n.01">Thus the superior man joins with his friends For discussion and practice.</apodosis>

<protasis wn_only="lake.n.01, evaporation.n.01">A lake evaporates upward and thus gradually dries up;</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="lake.n.01, replenishment.n.01">but when two lakes are joined they do not dry up so readily, for one replenishes the other.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="cognition.n.01, intercourse.n.01, friend.n.01, discussion.n.02, application.n.02, truth.n.01, life.n.01">It is the same in the field of knowledge. Knowledge should be a refreshing and vitalizing force. It becomes so only through stimulating intercourse with congenial friends with whom one holds discussion and practices application of the truths of life.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="learning.n.01, cheerfulness.n.01, lightness.n.05, learning.n.01, ponderousness.n.01">In this way learning becomes many-sided and takes on a cheerful lightness, whereas there is always something ponderous and one-sided about the learning of the self-taught.</apodosis>

THE LINES

<apodosis wn_only="remorse.n.01, disappearance.n.01">Remorse disappears</apodosis>.

Nine in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="joy.n.01, weight.n.01">Joyousness that is weighed</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="peace.n.01">is not at peace</apodosis>.
<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, mistake.n.01, riddance.n.01">After ridding himself of mistakes</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, joy.n.01">a man has joy</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, choice.n.01, weight.n.01, pleasure.n.01, kind.n.01">Often a man finds himself weighing the choice between various kinds of pleasures</protasis>, and <apodosis wn_only="decision.n.01, kind.n.01, peace.n.01">so long as he has not decided which kind he will choose, the higher or the lower, he has no inner peace</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="recognition.n.01, passion.n.01, suffering.n.01">Only when he clearly recognizes that passion brings suffering</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="mind.n.01, pleasure.n.01, endeavor.n.01">can he make up his mind to turn away from the lower pleasures and to strive for the higher</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="decision.n.01, seal.n.02">Once this decision is sealed</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="joy.n.01, peace.n.01, conflict.n.01">he finds true joy and peace, and inner conflict is overcome</apodosis>.

Nine in the fifth place means:
<protasis wn_only="sincerity.n.01,influence.n.01,danger.n.01">Sincerity toward disintegrating influences</protasis> is <apodosis wn_only="danger.n.01">dangerous</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="element.n.01,danger.n.01,man.n.01">Dangerous elements approach even the far best of men</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01,permission.n.01,influence.n.01,danger.n.01">If a man permits himself to have anything to do with them, their disintegrating influence acts slowly but surely, and inevitable brings dangers in its train</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01,recognition.n.01,situation.n.01,danger.n.01,protection.n.01">But if he recognizes the situation and can comprehend the danger, he knows how to protect himself and remains unharmed</apodosis>.


Six at the top means:

<apodosis wn_only="joyousness.n.01,seduction.n.01">Seductive joyousness</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="nature.n.01,vanity.n.01,pleasure.n.01">A vain nature invites diverting pleasures</protasis> and <apodosis wn_only="suffering.n.01">must suffer accordingly</apodosis> (cf. the six in the third place). <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01,instability.n.01,pleasure.n.01,world.n.01,influence.n.01">If a man is unstable within, the pleasures of the world that he does not shun have so powerful an influence that he is swept along by them</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="question.n.01,danger.n.01,fortune.n.01,misfortune.n.01,man.n.01,direction.n.01,life.n.01,chance.n.01,influence.n.01">Here it is no longer a question of danger, of good fortune or misfortune. He has given up direction of his own life, and what becomes of him depends upon chance and external influences</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, text.n.01">The text of this hexagram</protasis> resembles <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, gathering.n.01">that of Ts'ui, GATHERING TOGETHER</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="subject.n.01, element.n.01, separation.n.04">In the latter, the subject is the bringing together of elements that have been separated</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="water.n.06, lake.n.01, earth.n.01">as water collects in lakes upon the earth</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="subject.n.01, dispersion.n.02, dissolution.n.02, egotism.n.01">Here the subject is the dispersing and dissolving of divisive egotism</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="hexagram.n.01, way.n.04, gathering.n.01">DISPERSION shows the way, so to speak, that leads to gathering together</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="force.n.01, egotism.n.01, division.n.01">Religious forces are needed to overcome the egotism that divides men</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="celebration.n.01, feast.n.04, rite.n.01, family.n.01, state.n.01, ruler.n.01, union.n.01">The common celebration of the great sacrificial feasts and sacred rites, which gave expression simultaneously to the interrelation and social articulation of the family and state, was the means of employed by the great ruler to unite men</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="music.n.01, ceremony.n.01, emotion.n.01, heart.n.01, unison.n.01, consciousness.n.01, origin.n.01, creature.n.01">The sacred music and the splendor of the ceremonies aroused a strong tide of emotion that was shared by all hearts in unison, and that awakened a consciousness of the common origin of all creatures</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="disunity.n.01, rigidity.n.01, dissolution.n.03">In this way disunity was overcome and rigidity dissolved</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="cooperation.n.01, undertaking.n.01, goal.n.01, will.n.01, people.n.01, concentration.n.01">A further means to the same end is co-operation in great general undertakings that set a high goal for the will of the people; in the common concentration on this goal</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="barrier.n.01, dissolution.n.03, boat.n.01, stream.n.01, hand.n.01, task.n.01">all barriers dissolve, just as, when a boat is crossing a great stream, all hands must unite in a joint task</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="man.n.01, freedom.n.01, selfishness.n.01, consideration.n.01, perseverance.n.01, justice.n.01, steadfastness.n.01">But only a man who is himself free of all selfish ulterior considerations, and who perseveres in justice and steadfastness</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="capability.n.01, dissolution.n.03, hardness.n.01, egotism.n.01">is capable of so dissolving the hardness of egotism</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="dissolution.n.04, blood.n.01, dispersion.n.01, bloodshed.n.01, wound.n.01">The idea of the dissolving of a man's blood means the dispersion of that which might lead to bloodshed and wounds, i.e., avoidance of danger</protasis>.
<apodosis wn_only="man.n.01, difficulty.n.01, kin.n.01, danger.n.01">But here the thought is not that a man avoids difficulties for himself alone, but rather that he rescues his kin-helps them to get away before danger comes, or to keep at a distance from an existing danger, or to find a way out of a danger that is already upon them</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="lake.n.01, space.n.01">A lake occupies a limited space.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="water.n.06, lake.n.01, overflow.n.01">When more water comes into it, it overflows.</apodosis> Therefore <apodosis wn_only="restriction.n.01, water.n.06">limits must be set for the water.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="water.n.06, firmament.n.01">The image shows water below and water above, with the firmament between them as a limit.</protasis> <protasis wn_only="chinese.n.01, word.n.01, limitation.n.01, joint.n.01, bamboo.n.02, stalk.n.02">The Chinese word for limitation really denotes the joints that divide a bamboo stalk.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="life.n.01, parsimony.n.01, limit.n.01, outgo.n.01">In relation to ordinary life it means the thrift that sets fixed limits upon expenditures.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="morality.n.01, limit.n.01, superior.n.01, man.n.01, action.n.01, loyalty.n.01, disinterest.n.01">In relation to the moral sphere it means the fixed limits that the superior man sets upon his actions-the limits of loyalty and disinterestedness.</apodosis>

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="limitation.n.01,trouble.n.04">Galling limitation must not be persevered in.</protasis>

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="water.n.06, lake.n.01">Water over lake</protasis>: the image of <apodosis wn_only="limitation.n.01">LIMITATION</apodosis>.

Thus the superior man
<apodosis wn_only="creation.n.02, number.n.02, measurement.n.01">Creates number and measure</apodosis>,
And <apodosis wn_only="examination.n.01, nature.n.01, virtue.n.01, conduct.n.01">examines the nature of virtue and correct conduct</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="lake.n.01">A lake</protasis> is <apodosis wn_only="object.n.01, limitation.n.01">something limited</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="water.n.06">Water</protasis> is <apodosis wn_only="inexhaustibility.n.01">inexhaustible</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="lake.n.01, containment.n.01, amount.n.01, water.n.06, quantity.n.01">A lake can contain only a definite amount of the infinite quantity of water</protasis>; this is <apodosis wn_only="peculiarity.n.01">its peculiarity</apodosis>. In <protasis wn_only="life.n.01, human.n.01">human life</protasis> too the <apodosis wn_only="individual.n.01, significance.n.01, discrimination.n.01, limit.n.01">individual achieves significance through discrimination and the setting of limits</apodosis>. Therefore what concerns us here is <apodosis wn_only="problem.n.01, definition.n.01, discrimination.n.01, backbone.n.01, morality.n.01">the problem of clearly defining these discriminations, which are, so to speak, the backbone of morality</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="possibility.n.01, limitation.n.01, suitability.n.01, man.n.01">Unlimited possibilities are not suited to man</protasis>; <apodosis wn_only="life.n.01, dissolution.n.04, boundlessness.n.01">if they existed, his life would only dissolve in the boundless</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="strength.n.01, man.n.01, life.n.01, limitation.n.01, duty.n.01, acceptance.n.01">To become strong, a man's life needs the limitations ordained by duty and voluntarily accepted</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="individual.n.01, significance.n.01, spirit.n.01, freedom.n.01, limitation.n.01, determination.n.01, duty.n.01">The individual attains significance as a free spirit only by surrounding himself with these limitations and by determining for himself what his duty is</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="travel.n.01">Going</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="esteem.n.01">esteem</apodosis>.

If we seek to <protasis wn_only="restriction.n.01">impose restrictions on others only, while evading them ourselves</protasis>, these restrictions will always be <apodosis wn_only="resentment.n.01">resented</apodosis> and will <apodosis wn_only="resistance.n.01">provoke resistance</apodosis>. <apodosis wn_only="remorse.n.01">Remorse disappears</apodosis>.

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="wind.n.01, lake.n.01">Wind over lake</protasis>: the image of <apodosis wn_only="truth.n.02">INNER TRUTH</apodosis>.

Thus the <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01">superior man</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="discussion.n.02, criminal.n.01, case.n.01">discusses criminal cases</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="order.n.01, delay.n.01, execution.n.02">In order to delay executions</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="wind.n.01, water.n.06, penetration.n.02">Wind stirs water by penetrating it</protasis>. Thus the <apodosis wn_only="man.n.01">superior man</apodosis>, when <protasis wn_only="obligation.n.01, judgment.n.01, mistake.n.01, man.n.01">obliged to judge the mistakes of men</protasis>, tries to <apodosis wn_only="penetration.n.02, mind.n.01, understanding.n.01">penetrate their minds with understanding</apodosis>, in order to <apodosis wn_only="gain.n.02, sympathy.n.01, appreciation.n.01, circumstance.n.01">gain a sympathetic appreciation of the circumstances</apodosis>. In ancient China, the entire <apodosis wn_only="administration.n.01, justice.n.01">administration of justice</apodosis> was guided by this <apodosis wn_only="principle.n.01">principle</apodosis>. A deep <apodosis wn_only="understanding.n.01, pardon.n.01">understanding that knows how to pardon</apodosis> was considered the <apodosis wn_only="form.n.01, justice.n.01">highest form of justice</apodosis>. This <apodosis wn_only="system.n.01, success.n.01">system was not without success</apodosis>, for its <apodosis wn_only="aim.n.01, impression.n.01">aim was to make so strong a moral impression</apodosis> that there was no reason to <apodosis wn_only="fear.n.01, abuse.n.01, mildness.n.01">fear abuse of such mildness</apodosis>. For it sprang not from <apodosis wn_only="weakness.n.01">weakness</apodosis> but from a superior <apodosis wn_only="clarity.n.01">clarity</apodosis>.

<apodosis wn_only="echo.n.01, awakening.n.01, person.n.01, attraction.n.01">the echo awakened in men through spiritual attraction.</apodosis> <protasis wn_only="feeling.n.01, voice.n.02, truth.n.01, emanates from one's own heart.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="intention.n.01, effect.n.01, destruction.n.01">Any deliberate intention of an effect would only destroy the possibility of producing it.</apodosis> Confucius says about this line:

THE JUDGMENT
<protasis wn_only="modesty.n.01, conscientiousness.n.01">Exceptional modesty and conscientiousness</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="success.n.01, reward.n.01">are sure to be rewarded with success</apodosis>; however, if a man is not to throw himself away, it is important that they should not become <protasis wn_only="form.n.01, subservience.n.01">empty form and subservience</protasis> but <apodosis wn_only="dignity.n.01, behavior.n.01">be combined always with a correct dignity in personal behavior</apodosis>.

We must understand <protasis wn_only="demand.n.01, time.n.05">the demands of the time</protasis> in order <apodosis wn_only="offset.n.01, deficiency.n.01, damage.n.01">to find the necessary offset for its deficiencies and damages</apodosis>. In any event we must not count on <protasis wn_only="success.n.01">great success</protasis>, since <apodosis wn_only="strength.n.01">the requisite strength is lacking</apodosis>.

In this lies the importance of the message that <protasis wn_only="thing.n.12">one should not strive after lofty things</protasis> but <apodosis wn_only="thing.n.12">hold to lowly things</apodosis>. The structure of the hexagram gives rise to the idea that <protasis wn_only="message.n.01, bird.n.01">this message is brought by a bird</protasis>.

In Ta Kuo, PREPONDERANCE OF THE GREAT 28, <protasis wn_only="line.n.05">the four strong, heavy lines within, supported only by two weak lines without</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="image.n.01, ridgepole.n.01">give the image of a sagging ridgepole</apodosis>. Here <protasis wn_only="line.n.05">the supporting weak lines are both outside and preponderant</protasis>; this <apodosis wn_only="image.n.01, bird.n.01">gives the image of a soaring bird</apodosis>.

But <protasis wn_only="bird.n.01">a bird should not try to surpass itself and fly into the sun</protasis>; <apodosis wn_only="bird.n.01, earth.n.01, nest.n.01">it should descend to the earth, where its nest is</apodosis>. In this way <protasis wn_only="message.n.01, hexagram.n.01">it gives the message conveyed by the hexagram</protasis>.

THE IMAGE
<protasis wn_only="thunder.n.02, mountain.n.01">Thunder on the mountain</protasis>:


THE IMAGE of <apodosis wn_only="preponderance.n.01, small.n.01">PREPONDERANCE OF THE SMALL</apodosis>.

Thus in his conduct the superior man gives <apodosis wn_only="preponderance.n.01, reverence.n.01">preponderance to reverence</apodosis>.
In bereavement he gives <apodosis wn_only="preponderance.n.01, grief.n.01">preponderance to grief</apodosis>.
In his expenditures he gives <apodosis wn_only="preponderance.n.01, thrift.n.01">preponderance to thrift</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="thunder.n.02, mountain.n.01">Thunder on the mountain</protasis> is different from <protasis wn_only="thunder.n.02, plain.n.01">thunder on the plain</protasis>. <protasis wn_only="mountain.n.01, thunder.n.02">In the mountains, thunder</protasis> seems <apodosis wn_only="proximity.n.01">much nearer</apodosis>; <protasis wn_only="mountain.n.01, thunder.n.02">outside the mountains, it</protasis> is <apodosis wn_only="audibility.n.01, storm.n.01">less audible than the thunder of an ordinary storm</apodosis>. Thus the superior man derives an imperative from this image: he must always <apodosis wn_only="eye.n.01, duty.n.01, proximity.n.01">fix his eyes more closely and more directly on duty</apodosis> than does the ordinary man, even though this might make his behavior seem <apodosis wn_only="pettiness.n.01, world.n.08">petty to the outside world</apodosis>. He is <apodosis wn_only="conscientiousness.n.01, action.n.01">exceptionally conscientious in his actions</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="bereavement.n.01">In bereavement</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="emotion.n.01, ceremoniousness.n.01">emotion means more to him than ceremoniousness</apodosis>. In all his personal expenditures he is <apodosis wn_only="simplicity.n.01, unpretentiousness.n.01">extremely simple and unpretentious</apodosis>. In comparison with the man of the masses, all this makes him <apodosis wn_only="exceptionality.n.01">stand out as exceptional</apodosis>. But the essential significance of his attitude lies in the fact that <protasis wn_only="matter.n.01">in external matters</protasis> he is <apodosis wn_only="side.n.01, lowliness.n.01">on the side of the lowly</apodosis>.

<token id="chi_chi">
<protasis wn_only="transition.n.01, confusion.n.01, order.n.01">The transition from confusion to order is completed</protasis>, and <apodosis wn_only="object.n.01, position.n.01">everything is in its proper place even in particulars</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="line.n.01, position.n.01">The strong lines are in the strong places, the weak lines in the weak places</protasis>. <apodosis wn_only="outlook.n.01">This is a very favorable outlook</apodosis>, yet <apodosis wn_only="reason.n.01, thought.n.01">it gives reason for thought</apodosis>. THE LINES

Six at the beginning means:
<protasis wn_only="tail.n.01, water.n.06">He gets his tail in the water.</protasis>

<protasis wn_only="disorder.n.01, temptation.n.01, advancement.n.01, rapidity.n.01, accomplishment.n.01, tangibility.n.01">In times of disorder there is a temptation to advance oneself as rapidly as possible in order to accomplish something tangible.</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="enthusiasm.n.01, failure.n.01, humiliation.n.01, time.n.05, achievement.n.01, arrival.n.01">But this enthusiasm leads only to failure and humiliation if the time for achievement has not yet arrived.</apodosis> <apodosis wn_only="time.n.05, wisdom.n.01, opprobrium.n.01, failure.n.01, retention.n.01">In such time it is wise to spare ourselves the opprobrium of failure by holding back.</apodosis>

Nine in the second place means:
<protasis wn_only="brake.n.01, wheel.n.01">He brakes his wheels.</protasis>
<apodosis wn_only="perseverance.n.01, fortune.n.03">Perseverance brings good fortune.</apodosis>

Here again the time to act has not yet come. But the patience needed is not that of idle waiting without thought of the morrow. Kept up indefinitely, this would not lead to any success. Instead, an individual must develop in himself the strength that will enable him to go forward. He must have a vehicle, as it were, to effect the crossing. But he must for the time being use the brakes. <apodosis wn_only="patience.n.01, strength.n.01">Patience in the highest sense means putting brakes on strength.</apodosis> Therefore he must not fall asleep and lose sight of the goal. <protasis wn_only="strength.n.01, steadfastness.n.02, resolve.n.01">If he remains strong and steadfast in his resolve,</protasis> <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">all goes well in the end.</apodosis>

Six in the third place means:
<protasis wn_only="completion.n.01, attack.n.01">Before completion, attack</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="misfortune.n.01">misfortune</apodosis>.
It furthers one to <apodosis wn_only="crossing.n.01, body_of_water.n.01">cross the great water</apodosis>.

<protasis wn_only="time_period.n.01, transition.n.01">The time of transition</protasis> has arrived, but one <apodosis wn_only="lack.n.01, strength.n.01, completion.n.01, transition.n.01">lacks the strength to complete the transition</apodosis>. <protasis wn_only="attempt.n.01, force.n.02">If one should attempt to force it</protasis>, <apodosis wn_only="disaster.n.01">disaster would result</apodosis>, because <apodosis wn_only="collapse.n.01">collapse would then be unavoidable</apodosis>. What is to be done? <apodosis wn_only="situation.n.01">A new situation must be created</apodosis>; one must <apodosis wn_only="engagement.n.01, energy.n.01, helper.n.01, fellowship.n.01, step.n.01, crossing.n.01, body_of_water.n.01">engage the energies of able helpers and in this fellowship take the decisive step-cross the great water</apodosis>. Then <apodosis wn_only="completion.n.01, possibility.n.01">completion will become possible</apodosis>.

Nine in the fourth place means:
<protasis wn_only="perseverance.n.01">Perseverance</protasis> brings <apodosis wn_only="fortune.n.03">good fortune</apodosis>.
<apodosis wn_only="remorse.n.01, disappearance.n.01">Remorse disappears</apodosis>.
